Errors in Silver Needle Testing for Poison in "The Washing Away of Wrongs" 126

Forensic Institute's Investigation Deems It Impractical

Our country's examination of poisoning, according to "The Washing Away of Wrongs," involves inserting a silver needle into the corpse's mouth and anus, sealing it with paper, and removing it after a long time. It is said that if there is poisoning, the silver needle will turn dark black, and wiping it with soapberry water will not remove the discoloration. If there is no poisoning, the color will be bright white, and so on. Now, after investigation and experimentation by the Forensic Institute of the Ministry of Justice in Zhenru, it has been found that this method is absolutely impractical and has many errors. A request has been submitted to the Ministry of Justice, asking to instruct all levels of courts to comply. The original text is as follows:

Regarding the various articles on examining poisoning recorded in "The Washing Away of Wrongs," the method of inserting a silver needle into the corpse to determine whether it changes color to determine poisoning or not is impractical and has many errors. It is proposed to instruct compliance. The results of the experiments and opinions are listed below for your review.

The case of a criminal case is of utmost importance, and the examination of poison is especially important to be accurate and clear. Not only must the cause of death of the deceased be understood, but also the severity of the charges against the defendant, whether it concerns life or death. As for whether the poisoning is due to suicide, homicide, or accidental harm, and what kind of poison was taken, and what its ingredients are, it is also necessary to conduct a detailed examination, conduct a chemical test, or conduct a dissection experiment and an animal experiment to obtain accurate results and avoid wrongful convictions.

The specialized books in our country for examining corpses and injuries have always been compiled based on "The Washing Away of Wrongs." Legal officials regard "The Washing Away of Wrongs" and the "Collected Evidence Records" as the highest standards and guidelines. According to "The Washing Away of Wrongs," it started during the Chunxi era of the Song Dynasty when the judicial officer Song Ci collected and recorded the "Collection of Doubtful Cases" written by Jin He and Lu Gong Ning and his son, Prince Zhongyuan, and the "Inner Forgiveness Record" by an anonymous person in the Song Dynasty, and compiled them together. Among them, the various methods of examining injuries and poisons are divided into categories and seem to be described in detail without omission. However, in reality, there are many shortcomings. It has been followed to this day for more than 700 years. Unfortunately, the people of our country only know how to adhere to the old ways and stick to conventions. They lack scientific instruments to assist in the examination. Therefore, although many years have passed, there is no progress to speak of.

In modern times, science has reached a high level of development, and the methods of examining poisons are very complete. The types of poisons have increased, and the symptoms vary. If we continue to adhere to the old theories of "The Washing Away of Wrongs," and use soapberry water to wipe a silver hairpin, insert it into the mouth and anus of the dead person, seal it with paper and take it out after a long time, and say that the silver hairpin turns dark black, and wiping it again with soapberry water does not remove the color, and if it does not, its color is bright white, this is a major mistake. In fact, the result is not a sign of poisoning but a sign of corpse decomposition. According to the facts verified by this office, it can be proven that this method is very unreliable. When a person dies and the corpse decomposes, the stomach and intestines will especially decompose first. The corpse tissue and the contents of the intestines contain proteins that produce hydrogen sulfide due to decomposition. Hydrogen sulfide can cause a chemical reaction with silver. If a silver hairpin is used for testing, it will definitely turn black. If it is mistaken for poison, the error will be very serious. As for corpses, either because the stomach and intestines are empty, or because the degree of protein decomposition has passed, or because its effect is not very strong, the amount of hydrogen sulfide gas produced is very small. Often, the silver hairpin does not change color, or even if it changes color, it fades when washed. "The Washing Away of Wrongs" calls this "foul air," but in reality, it is due to the fact that there is too little sulfide combined with silver. As for arsenic, aluminum, salt, and various poisons, they cannot directly react with silver, that is, they cannot make the silver hairpin turn black. And feces and all decaying organic matter rich in protein, when heated and touched with silver, will turn black. This kind of fact has been verified by experimentation. Therefore, this experimental report is submitted to the public to dispel public doubts and eliminate wrongful imprisonment.

As for future cases of suspected poisoning in various places, it is hoped that the following five points will be followed to conduct examinations and investigations to clarify the situation:

(1) Investigate witnesses (the person themselves or others) to describe in detail the symptoms that occurred after the poisoning.

(2) Collect vomit, blood, stool, urine after poisoning, and even items stained with excretion stains.

(3) Collect suspected poisons, medicines, drinks, and food.

(4) Examine the symptoms of the poisoned patient or the deceased (preferably by a doctor).

(5) If the above items 1, 2, and 3 cannot be completely investigated and collected, then a corpse dissection should be performed to take the brain, heart, kidney, liver, lungs, stomach, intestines, and the contents of the stomach and intestines for chemical testing.

However, the materials collected for inspection in items 2, 3, 4, and 5 should be sent to a place with complete chemical equipment for chemical testing. General doctors do not have the knowledge of chemists, and hospitals do not have complete microscopic chemical qualitative and quantitative equipment, so it is not appropriate to be responsible for poison testing to avoid mistakes. Now that this office has been established for more than half a year, all books and instruments have been roughly set up. The poison testing facilities can be said to be sufficient. We can use the latest chemistry, toxicology, pathology, forensic chemistry, pharmacology chemistry, poison chemistry, electricity theory, and pharmaceutical equipment, as well as microscopes, spectrometers, ultraviolet analyzers, and other instruments, or animal experiments to help, no matter what kind of poison, we can carefully examine its nature, composition, toxicity, and harmful effects, and investigate its cause and effect. Therefore, in the future, if there are cases of suspected poisoning in various provinces, you can send the vomit, stool, urine of the poisoned person, or clothes and items stained with diarrhea, suspected poisons, drinks and food, or even the coffin, to this office for chemical testing according to the law. If the road is far away and transportation is inconvenient, and it is difficult to transport the coffin, you may wish to ask a doctor (local or nearby) to dissect the corpse nearby, take the internal organs such as the stomach and intestines, put them in bottles and seal them, and protect them with wooden boxes outside, and mail them to this office. You can also conduct chemical testing to clarify the situation and issue an appraisal letter for the basis of the judgment. However, the various articles on poison examination in "The Washing Away of Wrongs," the method of inserting a silver hairpin into the corpse is not a toxic reaction, it is extremely inapplicable, and it has been passed down in error, leaving a great impact. Now that the truth has been clarified, it should not be kept silent any longer, so that this false evidence of poisoning is still applied, and we sit idly by and watch the injustice. This is a great loss of the dignity of the law and goes against the correctness of public fairness. It is proposed that your department instruct all provinces and courts at all levels to comply with this instruction. The facts that the silver hairpin poison examination method in the "Washing Away of Wrongs" is impractical are written in the opinion letter and attached to this document for your review and instruction. It is indeed for the public good.

Trial Begins for Kidnapping of Child 127

Letter Demands 20,000 Yuan Ransom

Case Solved During Negotiation at Chinese-Foreign Hotel

A six-year-old boy, Atang, son of Jiang Desheng, a native of Shaoxing who resides at No. 45, Jianye Lane, Fulvli Road, in the French Concession and works at a branch office of the Shanghai Telephone Company on Bi Zhu Road, disappeared suddenly at 3:00 PM on February 13th while playing in the lane. Initially, it was thought that he had been abducted by bandits, and the French Concession police were notified to investigate. Later, Jiang received eight letters delivered by the post office, demanding a ransom of 20,000 yuan before the child would be released. It was then discovered that the child had been kidnapped. He repeatedly sent representatives to negotiate with the kidnappers, but without success. On the 16th of last month, detective Jin Jiulin of the Special Bureau of the French Concession Police learned that the kidnappers had arranged to negotiate the ransom at 9:00 PM that night in Room 21 of the Huayang Hotel on Guangxi Road in the Public Concession. He immediately led detectives Zhang Ziying, Zhou Yaoting, Zhou Bingcheng, Cui Zhendong, Cai Jinzhang, Qin Youyu, Zhang Chunsheng, and Xia Wanxing to the hotel at the appointed time. He successively apprehended the kidnappers Zhou Liansheng, Zhang Hualang, Fei Zhaojun, and Wang Desheng at Guangdong Road and Robert Road. He also rescued the hostage at No. 30, Wufuli, Tokyo Road, and apprehended the female kidnapper Qian Aizhen and Zhang Hexiang. (The male and female kidnappers were all natives of Shaoxing and from the same hometown as the victim). They were handed over to the Second Special District Court for public prosecution and interrogation. The details have been reported in previous newspapers. The police investigation has been completed, and yesterday morning, Judge Li Changnian ascended to the Criminal Court No. 1 to continue the trial of the defendants. First, Fei Xizhen, the lawyer for the police, described the police investigation in detail, stating that the police investigation has now revealed that the case was initiated by the fugitive Zhu Amao and the female bandit Zhang Guixian, the mother of the sixth defendant, Zhang Hexiang. With the consent of the third defendant, Fei Zhaojun, Zhang Guixian and Zhang Hexiang abducted the child to the Yadong Hotel on Guangdong Road at 3:00 PM on February 13th. Fei then escorted the child with Zhang Guixian and Zhang Hexiang to Qian Aizhen's house, the fifth defendant, at No. 30, Wufuli, Tokyo Road, for hiding, and left Zhang Hexiang there to guard the child. Later, Fei, on Zhu's orders, went to the corner of Baoding Road and Tangshan Road in Hongkou at 4:00 PM on March 14th to negotiate with the victim. The day before, Fei invited Zhou Liansheng and Zhang Hualang to participate in the negotiation. Because the ransom demanded was too high, there was no result. On the 16th, Fei and Zhou and Zhang made a second unsuccessful negotiation in front of the Yipinxing in Xizang Road. The victim's representative agreed to negotiate again at 9:00 PM that evening in the Huayang Hotel on Guangxi Road. At the appointed time, Fei accompanied Zhou and Zhang to the entrance of the hotel and left, allowing Zhou and Zhang to enter the door and talk with the victim's representative. The defendants were apprehended when the detectives learned of the situation and rushed to the scene. The police are now prosecuting the first, second, and third defendants under Article 372 of the Criminal Law for kidnapping and demanding ransom. The fourth defendant, Wang Desheng, confessed to having an affair with the fifth defendant, Qian Aizhen, but denied participating in the kidnapping. Therefore, the police are prosecuting the fifth defendant, Qian Aizhen, under Article 316 of the Criminal Law for illegal detention. Although the sixth defendant, Zhang Hexiang, is indeed guilty of the crime, she is still young and was instigated by her mother. The police are temporarily not prosecuting her and are requesting that the court make a ruling or send her to a charitable institution for education, etc.

Then, the victim Jiang Desheng testified that he suspected that his child had been abducted after he disappeared. He reported it to the police that night and requested an investigation. After receiving the letter, he knew that he had been kidnapped and immediately sent his neighbor Wei Bohua as a representative to negotiate with the bandits. He really had no money, so he agreed to pay 300 yuan to redeem the child, but the bandits wanted at least 1,500 yuan, so the negotiations were unsuccessful. The case was solved by the detectives, and the sixth defendant, Zhang Hexiang, and her mother had previously rented a house from our family, so they were familiar with each other, etc. The judge then ordered the defendants to be taken down and interrogated separately one by one. The defendants all admitted to the kidnapping and demanding ransom without denial. The interrogation was completed after noon, and the court ordered the case to be rescheduled for the 28th of this month to designate the person who needs money for further interrogation.

JIA BEI, TANZIWAN - Adulterer Kills and Wounds Husband 128

Shi Hangshi carried out three chops with a kitchen knife to Liu Yinsheng

At around 2:00 AM yesterday, Zhao Xinzhou, a police officer stationed at the Tanzhawan Sub-bureau of the Zhabei Fourth District Public Security Bureau, received a complaint from plaintiff Liu Laoda and his son Liu Yinsheng, claiming that Shi Hangshi's husband, Shi Hangshi, had used a kitchen knife to chop him on the head. Seeing Yinsheng covered in blood, the officer immediately went to investigate, but the assailant had already fled. He then took the assailant's wife, Hangshi, and Yinsheng's wife, Zhongshi, to the police station. After interrogation by Officer Lou, Liu Laoda stated that he was 48 years old, from Yixing, and lived at No. 113, Lane 7, next to the Dafeng Yarn Factory in Tanzhawan, making a living by farming. Tonight (i.e., yesterday morning), he and his son went to Hangshi's house to call his daughter-in-law, Zhongshi, home. After Yinsheng saw Zhongshi, they started arguing. Shi Hangshi gathered more than a dozen people to brutally beat his son. Shi Zhusan dared to wield a kitchen knife and chopped Yinsheng three times on the back of his head. Therefore, he brought Shi Hangshi to the bureau, but Shi Zhusan had already fled, etc. Liu Yinsheng stated that he was 25 years old and made a living by rowing a boat. His statement was similar to his father's, and he also stated that Shi Zhusan not only committed adultery with his wife, but when they were beating him, he said to Zhongshi, "You can beat me to death." Hangshi said, "I'll beat you to death," and Hangshi handed the kitchen knife to her husband, Shi Zhusan, who chopped him three times. Shi Hangshi stated that she was 38 years old and worked in a yarn factory. Liu Zhongshi was lodging and eating in her house. Today, her father-in-law and husband came to call her back. They had already walked out the door when she heard that something was wrong and then heard the sound of a knife. Yinsheng then shouted for help. She told her husband to chase after them, but they were brought to the bureau by the father and son. Liu Zhongshi stated that she was 20 years old. Today, her father and son came to call her, but she was already asleep. She told them that if they wanted her to go back to the countryside, they should pay off the money she owed here on her behalf. They said, "Where did your wages go?" Before she could finish speaking, they scolded her, ran outside, and took a kitchen knife and chopped herself several times on the head. The official verified the statements. As the case concerned injury, it should be sent to the Public Security Bureau for investigation along with the evidence after the documents are prepared.

Autopsy of Suicide Young Woman 129

Married Previously, Unhappily Divorced

Nervous Breakdown,厌世Suicide

Remains Coffined by Her Girlfriend

Chen Sufen, a modern young woman from Guangdong, went to the Hua'an Hotel on Jing'an Temple Road alone on the 13th of this month and rented Room 412. She was beautifully dressed, behaved luxuriously, and had a wide circle of friends. Therefore, male and female friends visited her every day. In the evening, the woman would often go out to banquets and not return until midnight. On the 16th, at midnight, the woman drove back to her residence from outside, and there was nothing unusual. But to her surprise, at 2:00 AM the next morning, after a male friend entered the room to visit her, he suddenly discovered that the woman had taken poison. The hotel staff immediately called a doctor for treatment, but the poison had entered her organs and could not be saved. She died at Baolong Hospital at 10:00 AM on the 17th. The hospital then notified the Xinzha Police Station, which sent detectives to take the body to the Philen Road autopsy center to await a coroner's examination. An investigation was conducted. The details were reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now known that detectives Zhang Yutian and Lu Gendi, who are handling the case, have learned from various investigations that the deceased, Chen Sufen, was 39 years old. She had been married in the past and had a daughter named Xiangling, who is now ten years old. However, because she did not get along well with her husband, she has divorced. Her father is still in her hometown in eastern Guangdong. The woman is young, although she has had setbacks in love, she is not willing to be submissive. She socialized everywhere and had many male friends. Among her belongings was a diary, which stated that a man named Rui Jin was one of the people she admired the most. Because Rui Jin had recently broken up with her, her words revealed a sense of disappointment. The diary also contained descriptions of her suicide, generally saying that she had a nervous breakdown, felt that life was meaningless, and therefore decided to commit suicide. In addition, there was a letter to her father, also saying that she had been planning suicide for a long time and that she was determined to carry it out this time, so please do not be sad. The detectives also learned that the wife of Yu Zhibo, a Cantonese resident at No. 10, Wanyi Lane, Luban Road, in the French Concession, was a close friend of the deceased. Yesterday morning, they reported to the First Special District Local Court Prosecutor's Office, and Prosecutor Guo Wei was appointed to visit the autopsy center for an examination. Yu Zhibo was specially summoned. According to Yu, the deceased often came to his house. Four days before the incident, she even stayed at his house for a day. He did not know anything else. The reporter then followed Prosecutor Guo into the corpse room and saw that the deceased's face was lifelike, only a red mark was found on her jaw. She was extremely beautiful. She was wearing a flannel coat and was barefoot and without shoes. After the examination, Guo said that since the deceased had no relatives in Shanghai, he ordered Yu Zhibo to sign a guarantee to claim the body for coffining. Yu then hired someone to go to the Wanguo Funeral Home to buy clothes and a coffin and immediately placed the body in it.

The Shanghai Citizens' Association for the Promotion of National Products considers this year to be the year of national products, an excellent opportunity to expand the national products movement, and to develop association affairs and concentrate the power of national products to save the country. Theatrical Thieves Shoot the victim in Hongqiao town, XUHUI 132

Zhang Zhonghua, a villager in Zhangjiaxiang, Hongqiao Town, Xuhui West Shanghai, makes a living by farming. His family is moderately wealthy. Recently, as his second daughter, Yue'e, is about to get married, Zhang and his wife were preparing her dowry, which attracted the attention of thieves. The previous night, Zhang returned home from drinking at a relative's house and had just fallen asleep when more than a dozen thieves speaking local dialects suddenly came outside the door, holding pistols, broke into the house. Zhang's whole family woke up in shock, but it was too late to escape. They were immediately monitored by the thieves and not allowed to make a sound. The thieves rummaged through chests and cabinets and searched arbitrarily. They slapped Zhang and his wife several times and demanded cash, forcing them to hand over the keys. Ms. Wang resisted slightly and was shot by a thief. The bullet entered from the left rib and did not penetrate. Seeing that they had caused trouble, the thieves immediately rushed out of the door and fled north. The place is six or seven miles away from the Hongqiao Town Police Station of the First Sub-bureau of the Sixth District. Moreover, that night was drizzly and exceptionally dark. By the time Police Chief Pan Xueceng led the police to arrive, the thieves had long gone. In total, silver dollars, clothing, and jewelry worth hundreds of yuan were looted. The victim has now submitted a list of losses and reported it to the police station in charge, requesting a thorough investigation. The injured Ms. Zhang Wang was rushed to Guangci Hospital for treatment. It is reported that the bullet entered her abdomen and has not yet been removed. Her life is feared to be in danger.

French Concession District Stall Locations 133

The French Concession Municipal Council has newly established regulations for managing street vendors and their stalls, with a license fee set at five yuan per month. The area for each vendor's stall must not exceed two meters in length and 1.2 inches in width, and must not occupy more than half the width of the sidewalk. The Health Department will also assign personnel to inspect goods at any time. Vendors who violate the regulations will be subject to a fine of one to ten yuan. Regulations also stipulate the areas where vendors can set up stalls. The following is a list of streets under the jurisdiction of each district police station where stalls are permitted: (Xiaodongmen Police Station District) Min Guo Road (from Xiaodongmen to Fujian Road), Jinliyuan Wharf (from Coach Yard to Xinkaihe); (Mailan Police Station District) Ningbo Road (from West Xinjiao Street to Mintiniyin Road), Zhengjia Muqiao Street (south side of Gongguan Road), Lao Beimen Road (south side of Gongguan Road), Tianzhutang Street (from Yongan Street to Min Guo Road), French Bund (from Gongguan Road to Xinkaihe); (Xiafei Police Station District) Lanwei'ai Road, Bai'er Road, Mintiniyin Road (from Ailai Ge Road to Milu Road, east side of Malang Road) Pingluo Road to Baxianqiao Vegetable Market, La Feide Road (east side of Ma Guo Road), Pingji Li Road (from Lai Gena Road to Lanwei'ai Road) Min Guo Road (from Pi Shaonai Road to Milu Road); (General Patrol Police Station District) Xujiahui Road, Father Du Road, Father Lao Road (east side of Sa Bocai Road), Bei Di'ao Road, Pu'en Jishi Road, Caishi Road, Kang Ti Road (east side of Lüban Road), Pu Shi Road (from Bei Di'ao Road to Bai'er Road); (Fuxu Police Station District) Pu Shi Road (from Gu Ba Road to Lao'er Dong Road), West Aixian Si Road (from Gan Shi Dong Road to La Du Road), Fu Lüli Road (from Ya'er Bei Road to La Du Road), Lao'er Dong Road (north side of Henry Road), Gan Shi Dong Road (from Lei Mi Road to West Aixian Si Road), Lei Mi Road (from Gan Shi Dong Road to La Du Road), Qianjia Tang Village (extension line of Huanlong Road); Xujiahui Road (Bei Dang Police Station District), Haige Road (between houses No. 1113 to 1169 and No. 1193 to 1279); Xujiahui Road (from tram terminus to Yao Zhujiao Road).

First Special Court Hearing of Three Theft Cases 134

Detective Wang Chengying of the Gordon Road Police Station, during the Western Spring Festival holiday, led detectives Pi Shaochang, Liu Xuecheng, Wu Wenxiang, etc., in solving three theft cases, which are summarized as follows: 1. On the night of April 13, the detectives first went to Room 12 of the Changzhou Inn on North Zhejiang Road, arrested a thief named Bao Yongkang, and found a pistol and five bullets. Then, in cooperation with the Zhabei Police Bureau, they successively arrested accomplices Bao Jinshan, Zhang Jingting, Wei Rongfu (i.e., Lao San), and Dai Hongying at No. 233 Nanlin Lane, No. 46 Tianbao Lane on Xinmin Road, and No. 71 Yuqing Lane, Tangjia Nong, at the Deteixin Inn on Zhejiang Road. Bao Jinshan had previously served as a member of the Zhabei Security Corps. According to Bao Yongkang, he borrowed the pistol from Bao Jinshan for self-defense. This morning, they were brought to the First Special Court for interrogation. Police lawyer Wang Yaotang requested an extension, stating that the case required further investigation of the crimes committed. Judge Qian approved the request and briefly questioned Bao and others, ordering a rescheduled hearing. 2. On the night of April 14, Detective Wang and others arrested a thief named Chen Degao, also known as Chen Yangshan, at the intersection of Route des Soeurs and Wuding Road, seizing two pistols and thirteen bullets from his person and right trouser leg. They then continued to arrest accomplices Wang Guangwu, Gu Naifu, Xu Da, Xu Zhenbiao, etc., seizing stolen goods including gold chain strips, gold lockets, and banknotes totaling one hundred and thirty yuan. Verdict in Lewd Monk's Premeditated Murder Case 135

Eighteen Years Imprisonment

Wang Nengjing, a lewd monk from Xinghua, seduced Liu, a recently widowed woman from his hometown, ten years ago. After committing adultery, he rented a house for them to live together, appearing as husband and wife. Around August of last year, the monk and the woman lived in the kitchen alcove at No. 68 Siwen Lane, Datong Road. At that time, the woman became romantically involved with Fan Weisheng, which aroused great jealousy in the monk. He specially purchased a sharp beef ear knife and, taking advantage of Wang's deep sleep one dark night, stabbed her to death. Fearing punishment, he fled. Recently, he secretly returned to Shanghai and resumed living with the woman at No. 9 Yongan Lane, Hengtong Road, Zhabei. Detective Feng Baishun of the Putuo Road Police Station detected his presence and arrested Nengjing. Together with Ouyang Liu, he was sent to the First Special District Local Court for interrogation. Yesterday morning was the sentencing date. Judge Qian Wenji ordered the defendant to be brought before the court for questioning about his name and background, then immediately announced the verdict: Wang Nengjing, for premeditated murder, is sentenced to eighteen years in prison. After the sentence was pronounced, he was taken back to the police station for detention, and will be sent to prison for execution after the sentence is finalized.

Judgment in Ship Leasing Lawsuit 138

| Tongyu Wins; Yadong to Compensate Various Amounts |

In October of the previous year, Yadong Shipping Company leased the Xin Ping An ship from Tongyu Shipping Company for a term of four months at a monthly rent of eight thousand yuan, with the delivery date set from November 20 to December 10 of the same year. Yadong manager Mo Zhaoyun then entered into a salt transportation contract with Deyi Xiang, using Xin Ping An to transport salt, with the loading date set to begin on December 12 of the same year. If the deadline was exceeded, Yadong would compensate Deyi Xiang four hundred yuan per day. However, Tongyu failed to deliver the ship as scheduled, and Yadong negotiated with them, but it was difficult to resolve. Subsequently, Yadong hired a lawyer to sue Tongyu for compensation for losses and outstanding payments, alleging that after entering into a contract with the plaintiff, the defendant Tongyu entered into another ship leasing contract with a third party, sending the Xin Ping An ship to Hong Kong, Shantou, Andong, Hongqi, and other places to transport coal, earning freight of twenty-three thousand four hundred and seventy-five yuan, causing the plaintiff to incur thirty-five thousand yuan in losses due to delayed salt transportation. Also, due to a daily overdue penalty of four hundred yuan, totaling fourteen days, the amount was five thousand six hundred yuan. In addition, not long after the ship was delivered, the Songhu Incident occurred, financial stagnation, so the second installment of rent could not be paid. The defendant used this as a reason to prohibit the ship from loading and unloading goods, from February 1 of last year to April 6, a total of sixty-six days, the ship was stopped in Jiujiang, unable to operate, counting from the date the defendant ordered the ship to stop, also forty-three days, calculated at four hundred yuan per day, a loss of seventeen thousand two hundred yuan. Also, because the defendant's Yuanda ship ran aground in Huangzhou, without obtaining the plaintiff's consent, the salt loaded on the Xin Ping An was unloaded, and the ship was sent to Huangzhou to tow the Yuanda, costing nine days. The plaintiff suffered a loss of seven thousand two hundred yuan. According to the lease, the ship should have expired on April 24 of last year, but the defendant arrived in Shanghai on April 19 and took it back without waiting for the expiration date, causing the plaintiff to suffer another two thousand yuan in damages. The plaintiff requested that the defendant be ordered to compensate for the above four items of loss in full and to declare provisional execution. The defendant then hired lawyer Shen Yuesheng to defend the case and filed a counterclaim against Yadong. The reasons for the defense were to refute each of the plaintiff's claims, stating that the various losses claimed by the plaintiff were completely unfounded and that the defendant could not admit them. As for the facts of the counterclaim, it stated that the rent payable by the plaintiff Yadong Company to Tongyu and the price of coal purchased on its behalf totaled thirty-three thousand two hundred and fifty-four yuan, five jiao, and three fen. After receiving it, deducting the fifteen thousand six hundred and forty-three yuan, six jiao, owed to the defendant, the plaintiff requested that the Yadong Company be ordered to repay the amount in full and pay interest. After repeated hearings by Li Hu, the civil division chief of the First Special District Local Court, summoning both parties for interrogation, the court recognized that the plaintiff Yadong Shipping Company's claims were completely unreasonable and rejected its suit. The defendant Tongyu Shipping Company's counterclaim against Yadong, with ample evidence, was upheld by special judgment, ordering Yadong to repay Tongyu one thousand, five thousand, six hundred, forty-three yuan, and six jiao, as well as interest at an annual rate of 5% from December 20 of last year until the date of execution. The costs of both the main suit and the counterclaim shall be borne by the plaintiff.

Chen Qiaonian Murder Case: Daughter-in-Law Acquitted 142

| Court Issues Decision Not to Prosecute |

On March 20 of this year, a case of a son and daughter-in-law plotting to murder an elderly father occurred in Shijia Lane, Nanshi. The deceased, an elderly man named Chen Qiaonian, was murdered, with a hemp rope tied around his neck and a knife wound on the back of his head. After investigation by the police, he was rescued and survived. It was then reported that he had been murdered by his eldest son, Chen Kaihong, daughter-in-law Chen Yang, and second son, Chen Xiaogou. The police station dispatched officers to arrest Chen Kaihong and others and send them to the local court for interrogation, trial, and detention pending investigation. Details have been previously reported. It has now been learned that the case was investigated by Prosecutor Zheng Qinming, and the results showed that the defendants had absolutely no murderous intent. A decision was made not to prosecute, and Chen Kaihong, Chen Xiaogou, Chen Yang, and others who were detained were released on bail some days ago. The facts and reasons for the decision not to prosecute are summarized as follows: Chen Kaihong and Chen Xiaogou are the sons of Chen Qiaonian, and Chen Yang is Chen Kaihong's wife. On February 24 of this year, Qiaonian wanted to go to Nanjing, and Kaihong and Xiaogou jointly gave him eight yuan for travel expenses. Qiaonian used up all the money and did not go. That night, he secretly stayed on a boat by the river. The next day, he wandered around Puxi. At 9:00 PM, he passed by Shijia Lane in Nanshi and was tied up with a rope. The case was submitted by the Public Security Bureau. After investigation and interrogation, it was found that the defendants were all working in Pudong that day, and Chen Yang was at home breastfeeding. There was no act of murder. This shocking case of filial impiety has thus come to a close.

Reader's Consultant 152

A Collection of Letters Discussing the Question of "Can We Return to the Countryside?"

(12) Letter from Mr. Yu Yuesheng of this city! Where shall we go?

On April 5th, in the Shanghai News Reader's Consultant column, there was Mr. You Huai’s response to Mr. Xiongsheng's discussion "Can We Return to the Countryside?". After reading it, I felt very disappointed. Mr. You's reply was not only irrelevant, but also extremely dangerous. First, it inverted the facts, and second, it made the problem unrealistic, turning it into a utopia, desperately escaping reality. He said, "I (Mr. You) feel that in times of national crisis, seeing the drunken and dreamlike life in the city, it is better to find a quiet and lovely countryside to find another way out, relying on my ability, and spend ten years to build a new kind of Arcadia in my mind." This fully shows that Mr. You does not understand the current society, especially the "countryside", otherwise he would not have said such things. We will not talk about the theory for the time being, just talk about the facts. Thousands of farmers are leaving their homes and constantly moving to the cities. Is this because they don't "love the countryside"? Do they not love their "farmer friends (relatives) in the countryside"? Or is it because they "are not determined to work hard and seek a life in the countryside"? (This is Mr. You's "prerequisite for going to the countryside") No, no, it's entirely because they can't live in the countryside, live a normal life! Why can't they live in the countryside? This is a problem of the current society, just like we can't live in the city. Then, the question of "Can we return to the countryside?" is very clear. Since neither the countryside nor the city has a way for us to live, where shall we go? Suicide? Sit and wait for death? Of course, we are unwilling. Then, is there still a way to go? Yes, it is to actively fight for our survival. Fighting for survival cannot be achieved by empty talk, nor can it be achieved by "relying on my (personal) ability" (personal strength is very weak in the current society, it can only be achieved by the common struggle of the majority of people who cannot survive but want to survive! The main thing is to solve the contradictions under the current social system, so that we can survive. Not only in the countryside, but also in the city, there is a way for us to live.

(13) Letter from Mr. Wei Hao of this city! Discussing the rural issues with Mr. You Huai Gao

After reading Mr. You's letter, I realized that Mr. You is originally a dreamer. The prerequisites he said for going to the countryside, (1) Do you love the countryside, there are some questions about this. Mr. Xiongsheng was originally from the countryside, and he had to go to the city for a living. Now, because of unemployment, he plans to return to the countryside. The fact tells us that under the current system, the only hope is a stable life, not a matter of love or not. As long as there is a place to live, whether it is a city or a countryside, (2) Do you sincerely love your farmer friends in the countryside, regarding this point, I don't know whether Mr. Xiongsheng sincerely loves them or not. However, Mr. Xiongsheng has already expressed, "There is nothing in the city that makes me nostalgic." Of course, he can only jump out of this city and go to the countryside. Farmers have no complaints, and naturally there is no reason not to love them, but sincerely loving farmer friends cannot solve the problem of life, so what? As for the advantages of the countryside, (1) and (2) are acceptable, and (3) being more free in life, this is Mr. You's dream. In fact, is it better than in the city? The authority of local tyrants and evil gentry can make farmers suffer and dare not speak out at any time. On the level of suffering in the countryside, it is true that sufficient enjoyment cannot be obtained in terms of material things, but how can a penniless person living in the city enjoy material things? Moreover, Mr. Xiongsheng is unemployed, and his life is still a problem, so there is no talk of enjoyment. Mr. You also said that people who have lived in the city for a long time may feel bored and boring. This is not for Mr. Xiongsheng, but for two wealthy people to think deeply. Mr. You thinks that "in this time of national crisis, it is better to find a quiet and lovely countryside to find another way out, and spend ten years to build a new kind of Arcadia in my mind." Mr. You is simply not solving the difficulties for Mr. Xiongsheng, but writing an ideal article for himself. May I ask, in the current situation of rural bankruptcy, how can a penniless Mr. Xiongsheng build a "new Arcadia"? Mr. You is really too smart, thinking that now that the country is in trouble, the only way is to escape to the countryside to build Arcadia. Then the suffering compatriots in the four northeastern provinces should all have a way out, and they will not be slaughtered by Japanese imperialism, right? Mr. You said, "The city lacks food and materials, which can be supplied by the countryside." That's right, the production in the countryside is enough to supply the needs of the city, but since capitalism has poisoned the countryside in China, not only the city lacks, there is no need to rely on the countryside, but the current countryside is also being messed up by capitalism. Talking about Mr. You's first step in teaching Mr. Xiongsheng, the content seems to be not bad, but with Mr. Xiongsheng's poverty, it is really not easy to raise one or two hundred yuan. Moreover, in the years of economic bankruptcy in rural China, the primary problem for farmers! Life, is still not solved, making their children receive education, as far as I know, it is simply impossible, and the tuition and difficulty in reading make it even more difficult. If Mr. Xiongsheng is a rich man, such a losing business may be okay to play with as a pastime. Mr. You's second step is also not bad, but if the first step doesn't work, then the second step, under the current chaotic situation of natural disasters, man-made disasters, and harsh taxes, will not have any results. Mr. You's third step is to practice medicine and sell medicine. Regarding this point, the doctor registration statistics of the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau can show that it is not a successful thing. In the past two years, there has been a surplus of doctors in Shanghai, but the reason is that too many people from the inland have come to Shanghai to make a living. Then, what certainty does Mr. Xiongsheng, who is an outsider to medicine, have to go to the countryside? Mr. You's fantasy is unrealistic, which eventually leads to the ideal of the fourth step of "carrying out village governance work". I think the first three are simply impossible, and the fourth one has no basis, but Mr. You is enthusiastic about advocating rural education to save the country. I don't know what the content is. I hope Mr. You can give us a chance to read a long article. Finally, according to my personal opinion, Mr. Xiongsheng is unemployed in the city and returning to the countryside, it is the same. Weather Report 156

The Xujiahui Observatory announced at 4:30 pm yesterday that the weather around Shandong is sunny with a gentle northeast wind. The weather in the Yangtze River Basin is cloudy, mostly cloudy, with fog or local showers. The wind comes from the northeast to the southeast. Important News 157

Measures for Donating Money to Purchase Aircraft by the Shantou Education Community

(Shantou Correspondence) The Guangdong Education Department has decided on the measures for donating money to purchase aircraft by the education community, one named Guangdong Student and one named Guangdong Education. The Shantou Municipal Government has received detailed measures for donating money and has specially ordered all public and private primary and secondary schools in the city to handle it quickly, and remit and submit it to the Department before the end of the month. The measures for donating money by each school are as follows: 1. Primary school students donate one hao each time (the following are all at once). 2. Middle school students donate one yuan. 3. Students above specialized schools donate two yuan. 4. Primary school teachers donate one yuan. 5. Middle school teachers and staff donate 5% of their monthly salary. 6. Teachers and staff above specialized schools and administrative agencies donate 10% of their monthly salary. All the above donations are calculated in hao yang.

Joint Conference of Wuxi County Schools 159

The Wuxi County School Federation held its 13th membership meeting at 1 pm yesterday at Meicun County Fourth Primary School. The chairman was Yan Shaoling. The abstracts of the important cases resolved are as follows: 1. The new curriculum standards will be implemented in primary and secondary schools, and whether the admission test questions and curriculum of public and private senior and junior high schools can be closely linked with the new curriculum standards is a major issue. How should we make suggestions to the higher authorities to benefit students' further education? It was resolved that the association should submit a request to the Education Bureau and forward it to the Education Department, ordering all public and private senior and junior high schools to pay attention to closely linking the curriculum and admission test questions with the new curriculum standards in the future. 2. In recent years, the level of living has been increasing, and the treatment of primary school teachers in county schools has become increasingly meager. If this continues, they will not be able to maintain their living needs and will leave their primary school teaching positions. How should we find ways to improve their treatment to benefit primary school education? It was resolved that (A) the association should submit a request to the Education Bureau to appropriately increase the standard fees for county school classes when preparing the next year's budget to improve treatment. (B) It was handed over to the Executive Committee for handling. 3. The association should find a way to request that various secondary schools not use classical Chinese exams when recruiting new first-year junior high school students. It was resolved that the association should submit a request to the Education Bureau and forward it to the Education Department, ordering all public and private secondary schools not to test classical Chinese when recruiting new first-year junior high school students. 4. Submit a request to the Education Bureau of the County Government and forward it to the Provincial Education Department, requesting the Ministry of Education to investigate the amount of public funding occupied by each student in each primary school in each province, city, and county across the country each year, in order to clarify the efficiency of primary school education. The resolution was passed. 6. Submit a request to the Education Bureau of the County Government and forward it to the Provincial Government Education Department, ordering the consolidation of the city root base in this county to enrich the county education funds. The resolution was passed. Other cases are omitted.

The County Government Meeting Revised the Measures for Compulsory Education 160

The Shanghai County Government held its 145th county government meeting yesterday. The chairman was County Magistrate Tang. The meeting was held as usual. First, the chairman reported that the county government meeting would be held as usual, and no notice would be issued afterwards. If a temporary county government meeting is convened, or if it is not held due to circumstances, a separate notice will be given at any time. Secondly, the county magistrate discussed and resolved the plan for the implementation of compulsory education in public schools submitted by the County Education Bureau. 1. The end of item 7 of the original plan was revised to be: the school may send a letter to the local public security bureau to collect a dereliction fine of three yuan or less and still order enrollment. The aforementioned dereliction fine shall be refunded if enrollment is complied with; otherwise, it shall be confiscated. 2. This plan shall be submitted to the Education Department for approval before implementation.

The French Concession Authorities Forced the Closure of Schools Yesterday 161

Nangshang Bowen Club classes as usual

Morning Glow and other schools are still in negotiations

丨The Municipal Education Bureau Submits a Report to the Municipal Government for Instructions丨

(Central News Agency) Bowen Girls' Middle School, Morning Glow Girls' Middle School, and Nanyang Commercial High School in the French Concession have recently been ordered to close down immediately by the French Concession Public Works Bureau because they are deemed to have insufficient facilities. The school authorities have all registered with the Municipal Education Bureau, and this move is obviously undermining the integrity of our educational administrative power. Therefore, they have submitted a request to the Municipal Education Bureau to negotiate. The reporter inquired with the Municipal Education Bureau yesterday and learned that the Bureau Director Pan Gongzhan expressed his indignation at the French Concession authorities' interference in our educational administrative power beyond their authority and has reported the details to the municipal government for instructions. It is also learned that the French Concession authorities have also withdrawn the order after explanations from various parties.

(Shanghai News Agency) Regarding the French Concession authorities' forcing the closure of Morning Glow Girls' Middle School and other schools in the concession, the Shanghai News Agency reporter learned about the situation from various parties yesterday, which is slightly different from what was reported yesterday. The details are as follows:

Nanyang High School of Commerce Nanyang Commercial High School, which was moved to Shanzhong Road in the French Concession after the January 28th Shanghai War, said yesterday that the school secretary Mao Zhaorong said that the school had been registered with the Municipal Education Bureau. The school building was destroyed after the Shanghai War and moved here. Although it is temporary in nature, the school building is spacious and the facilities are adequate, and there is nothing wrong with it. Now that no closure order has been received from the French Concession authorities, nor have they seen anyone sent to the school to prevent classes. The school has never had a suspension of classes. Now that it is reported in the newspaper, I am afraid there is a misunderstanding. The health license for February has already been issued. The school's Dean of Academic Affairs, Dr. Wu Jiang Leng, personally visited Director Lai of the Health Department today. Lai said that there was no such thing and asked the French Public Works Bureau and said that it was all rumors.

Bowen Girls' Middle School Furthermore, Ms. Huang Zhaolan, the principal of Bowen Girls' Middle School, told reporters that the school was established seventeen years ago and was the first batch of schools registered with the Municipal Education Bureau in the seventeenth year. It was also filed with the Ministry of Education. How the school has been managed since then is well known to the community. The report that the French Concession authorities forced the school to close down is not true. The students of the school are still attending classes as usual and are at peace with each other. Today, a special envoy from the French Public Works Bureau came to the school to explain and requested a correction. It is said that there was a misunderstanding. However, one side of the lead-sheet school sign at the entrance of the school was suddenly stolen last night, which is very strange. Morning Glow Girls' Middle School The reporter went to Morning Glow Girls' Middle School to meet Principal Xue of the school. According to him, a detective suddenly came to the school on the 11th of this month and verbally notified them to stop classes. The school felt that the matter was strange and went to the French Public Works Bureau to inquire the next day. The Director General of the Bureau said that the school was unsanitary and should be improved, but he did not explain why it was unsanitary. He requested that the Bureau send someone to investigate. On the 13th, the Director General of the Health Department came to the school, took a look at it occasionally, and said that the playground must be paved with yellow sand and the ceiling must be painted. The school immediately complied with the instructions and completed it completely. However, there has been no reply approving the resumption of classes.

Other Schools Other schools such as Wenguang Primary School, Yihua Primary School, Xingzhong Primary School, Xinlai Primary School, Yixin Primary School, Jintong Primary School and other six schools were all stopped from attending classes by one or two detectives, and no official order was issued.

University League Issues a Letter to Allied Nations of the World Regarding the Sino-Japanese Problem 162

The Far East Problem is the Biggest Cause of World Disputes

The Washington Conference Should Unanimously Sanction Japan's Atrocities

The Shanghai University Student Union, because the Washington Conference is about to open, and the Sino-Japanese problem will also be discussed at the conference, specially decided to issue a letter to the Allied Nations of the World at the last inaugural meeting, stating the opinions of Shanghai students on the recent international situation and the Sino-Japanese problem. The declaration has been drafted and is now being translated into English, German, French, and Japanese to be broadcast to all countries in the world. The following is an excerpt of the original Chinese manuscript:

In order to realize its East Asia Doctrine and deepen the colonization of China, Japanese imperialism has spared no effort to abandon international trust, commit great unrighteousness, violate the Kellogg-Briand Pact, the League of Nations Covenant, and the Washington Nine-Power Treaty, and implement armed occupation of our three northeastern provinces to create the "Manchukuo Puppet State", which triggered the Shanghai War. Recently, it has become more and more greedy, ignoring the resolution of the League of Nations General Assembly, implementing withdrawal from the League, and sending troops to occupy Jehol. Moreover, it still cannot satisfy its greed, and continues to expand its military operations against us, gradually attempting to occupy North China and sweep through Tianjin. Our government and people have always taken the protection of peace and the upholding of the dignity of international treaties as their duty. Therefore, after the disaster occurred, we immediately requested arbitration from the League of Nations. Although the report of the League of Nations Investigation Team suggested a plan to resolve the Sino-Japanese dispute, China stood in the position of being invaded and was not willing to recognize it. However, for the sake of world peace and Eastern peace, our government is still willing to compromise and has accepted it in principle. The report of the Special Committee of Nineteen Nations, which is based on the Lytton Report, was also passed at the League of Nations General Assembly because of China's sincerity in maintaining peace. Now that the League of Nations' proposal to resolve the Sino-Japanese dispute based on Article 15 of the Covenant has failed because Japan refused to accept it and withdrew from the League, then the responsibility for destroying peace should be borne solely by Japan, which has added another layer of evidence. From the beginning, the countries involved in the Sino-Japanese dispute were China and Japan, and the League of Nations was in the position of mediation and arbitration. Now, the object of the dispute has replaced China's position with the League of Nations. If the League of Nations can still fulfill its responsibility to maintain international "justice" and "peace", then the countries participating in the League of Nations, especially the major countries that preside over the League of Nations, should immediately invoke Article 16 of the Covenant to impose sanctions on Japan. This is a matter of course. However, after the report of the Special Committee was passed, the League of Nations has taken no other action except to start the organization of the Twenty-Nation Committee and invite the United States and Russia to participate in the joint study of solutions to the Liaoning case. Even when discussing the prohibition of exporting munitions to belligerent countries, our representative Gu Weijun proposed that the principle of prohibiting the export of munitions should be stipulated for aggressor countries and invaded countries, but the conference ignored it. Then, after the report of the Special Committee was established, Japan brazenly ignored everything and continued its military oppression against us, swept through Jehol, and threatened Tianjin. There is a reason for this. However, just as Japan's military oppression against us is deepening, it happens to be the time when international disputes in Europe are expanding. The German-French situation, the Four-Power Agreement, and the disarmament issue have made the United Kingdom, France, Italy, and Germany too busy to deal with their own problems, and they have no energy to consider the Eastern problem. The debt dispute is also a stumbling block to European and American cooperation. If this problem can be temporarily resolved, then the United Kingdom, France, the United States, and other countries will unite in the Far East to sanction Japan, which is also impossible in fact. To solve the Eastern dispute, we must first seek cooperation between Europe and the United States, and to seek cooperation between Europe and the United States, we must first solve the internal disputes in Europe. From the current international situation, we also admit this point and are painstakingly trying to mediate the matter. Now, the Washington Conference is about to open in Washington, and the Far East problem will also be listed as one of the discussion topics. China and Japan have also accepted the invitation to participate. However, we would like to represent all Shanghai students here to contribute to our allied friends that the Far East problem is the biggest factor in world disputes, and the brutal policies of the Japanese warlord government are the biggest source of international peace. If this is not sanctioned, then the international crisis will never be eliminated. Today's countries are all part of the entire international community. The shattering of one ring will affect the whole situation. The Far East problem and the German problem are the two major centers of international problems after the European War. If this is not resolved, international peace will never be established. Now that the Washington Conference has gathered the leaders of the world's major countries in one place, its power to guarantee peace and sanction Japan is greater than the League of Nations Conference. Moreover, the disputes among the countries themselves will be dispelled at this Washington Conference, so it is even more possible to unanimously sanction Japan's policy of aggression. The dawn of world peace will depend on this Washington Conference, and the success or failure of the conference will depend on the resolution of the Far East problem. The times are difficult and the responsibility is heavy. May our allied governments and people take this into consideration. School. The detectives rushed into the classroom on their own and announced to the students that foreigners were on holiday for Qingming Festival today, so the students left the school one after another. In short, the procedure for the French authorities to deal with the school's closure this time is quite ridiculous and laughable.

Request for Negotiations The Municipal Education Bureau has only received written reports from Morning Glow Yihua and other four schools regarding the French Concession authorities' closure of private schools. Since the remaining schools have not submitted reports, the situation is not very clear. The facts of each school that has already reported have been forwarded to the municipal government for review. The Root Cause of This Matter According to the results of the reporter's inquiries from various parties, the root cause of the French Concession authorities' resolute action this time is actually due to the organization of the French Concession Private School Federation, which requested subsidies for private schools in the concession, which aroused the dissatisfaction of the French Concession authorities. As a result, an investigation of the schools was conducted, which led to today's incident.

216km Shanghai-Hangzhou Long-Distance Race, Huang Shengbai First 168

First to Arrive in Hangzhou at 12:53:12 PM Yesterday

Total Time for the Four-Day Journey Was 21 Hours, 21 Minutes, and 27 Seconds

| Li Yagu Second, Zhou Ruquan Third, Six Reached Within the Specified Time |

The Shanghai-Hangzhou long-distance race, initiated by the Baihong Athletic Team, departed from Shanghai on the 14th and arrived in front of the English statue on the shores of West Lake in Hangzhou at 12:53:11 PM yesterday. The first place winner was Huang Shengbai, with a total time of 21 hours, 21 minutes, and 27 seconds for the four-day journey. Second place went to Li Yagu, and third to Zhou Ruquan. A total of six people arrived within the specified time. Seventeen people started, and seven dropped out along the way. Details are recorded below:

From Hai'ning to Hangzhou 169

(Special Dispatch from Hangzhou) The Baihong team's Shanghai-Hangzhou long-distance race, after lodging in Haining on the evening of the 17th, showed spirited faces at dawn on the 18th. The previous night, the sky was full of stars, but unexpectedly, heavy rain came in the middle of the night and continued until the 8:30 AM departure. There were thirteen participants starting out, but six had already dropped out. About 11 kilometers from Haining, Huang Shengbai and Zhou Ruquan took the lead, with Li Yagu and Bao Yibi trailing by over 400 meters. The remaining runners were spaced about 3-4 meters apart. The last place was shared by Wu Shuying and Zhu Shengyuan, who both withdrew before reaching Wengjiabu. At Wengjiabu, Zhou Ruquan and Huang Shengbai were neck and neck, with Li Yagu trailing by about 800 meters, as was Chai Huanjin. Bao Yibi was about the same distance behind Chai. As a result of the intense competition, Huang Shengbai took first place, and Li Yagu took second. Li made a final sprint to the finish line, astonishing onlookers. From Qintai Gate to the Chen Yingshi statue on the shores of West Lake, fifty members of the Zhejiang Provincial Boy Scouts Fifth Regiment (orphanage) were stationed at various posts, wearing bamboo hats, holding Baihong flags, and showing great spirit, undeterred by the wind and rain, comparable to the racers. The Hangzhou Postal Workers' Union presented a large silver shield, which we heard was internally designated to be awarded to Chai Huanjin. The principal of Hangzhou Senior High School visited the hotel and gifted several cakes as a gesture of慰勞.

Details of the Intense Competition Along the Way

Three Quit Before Reaching Minhang - After arriving at Minhang, they crossed the river one after another. Chen Xuzhou was the first to reach Nanqiao, took a brief refreshment break, and then continued forward, reaching his destination at 1:49:05 PM, taking only 5 hours, 19 minutes, and 5 seconds, including the river crossing and refreshment break. Following him were Huang Shengbai, Li Yagu, Jin Zhongkang, and Zhou Ruquan. About a mile from Longhua, Kuang Shihuai withdrew onto the ambulance because he had injured his foot during practice, and his old injury recurred, leaving him no choice but to give up. Zhu Shengyuan and Meng Guangyi, due to hunger, went to find food and missed the time, taking a car to Caojing. However, the staff waiting in Minhang were greatly inconvenienced, waiting until 5:00 PM without seeing them arrive.

Xie and He Stop After Crossing Zhapu - After arriving at Caojing, they went to the hotel. Fortunately, the local Public Security Bureau sent people to prepare, and although the place was crude, there was nothing else they could do. They got up at dawn, had breakfast, and set off at 7:40 AM. The weather was terrible, with a slight breeze blowing incessantly, and drizzling rain falling non-stop. When they reached the Jin Siniang Bridge, the rain suddenly intensified and became torrential, and they were all soaked to the bone. Upon reaching Zhapu, the weather cleared up, and the racers became like furnaces, using their own body heat to dry their clothes. Chen Xuzhou was again the first to arrive. Before crossing Zhapu, Xie Guolue withdrew, and after crossing Zhapu, He Dafu did the same. At 1:41:10 PM, people from Haiyan met Chen Xuzhou on the seashore, and the county Party headquarters, farmers' association, women's association, chamber of commerce, district office, and other seven groups prepared refreshments and presented brocade flags, which was quite a scene.

Chen Xuzhou Switches to Riding a Bicycle - It was originally planned to go to Haining on the 16th, but there was heavy rain all night on the 15th, and the sea breeze added to the ferocity, which did not stop until 8:00 AM the next morning. The referees, out of consideration for the racers and to prevent them from getting sick, ordered a halt, but with the condition that they had to continue the next day no matter the weather. At 8:00 AM sharp on the 17th, they departed from Haiyan in a light breeze and drizzle. Lin Quanbo reluctantly withdrew due to food issues. Chen Xuzhou and Xu Yanbo stopped halfway. Zhou Ruquan was the first to arrive at Jiaoliyan, where the teachers and students of the local elementary school came to visit and took a group photo with Zhou Ruquan upon his arrival. After passing Jiaoliyan, Chen Xuzhou suddenly got off the ambulance and switched to riding a bicycle, leading Zhou and Huang all the way to Haining, and leaving Huang Shengbai more than 3,000 meters behind. It is strange that he can ride a bicycle but refuses to run.

Amateur Group A Billiards, Medina Advances to the Quarterfinals 171

Wins Peckar 1000 Points to 811

Li Gongying vs. Xu Shizhang Today

Chunqiu (Spring and Autumn)

Talking About Human Relationships 173

— Guo Lanxin

Last night at the Xinya Restaurant, I was drinking with my classmate Jun Shaoyou, whom I hadn't seen for three years. In his drunkenness, I heard him say some sorrowful words about the state of the world and human relationships. He said, "Ah, when I was in school, I was very young, and I felt hopeful about everything. Brightness and happiness were like two bright lights shining in front of me. At the same time, my family was well-off, and many relatives and friends were very affectionate. But since my family went through many changes two years ago, and both my parents passed away one after another, all my property has been scattered and exhausted in several changes. As a result, those relatives and friends have become distant. When people asked for my help, I tried my best to provide it to them, feeling that people should help each other. At that time, people would flatter and fawn over me. Now that I need people's help, they seem to have made an agreement to quietly distance themselves from me. I am still the same person I was before, but people treat me completely differently. Now I understand that their flattery and fawning at that time were not for me as a person, but merely in the hope of achieving their material assistance. Now that the hope of material assistance is gone, they no longer flatter and fawn. I have now gained a new experience and lesson: Human beings are __________, they are only a combination of interests."

After listening to his words, I felt that in this materialistic era, human warmth and the coldness of the world are exposed everywhere. This has already become a common phenomenon. The words "there is no mutual assistance among human beings, only a combination of interests" were particularly poignant and accurate. Wherever there are interests, people will cling to the powerful and engage in deceitful scheming, and even family members will clash and break apart, not to mention relatives and friends. Is this also a transformation of the world and people's hearts!

Doing One Thing, Complaining About It 174

— Baihe

"Doing one thing, complaining about it." The old man worked as a barber and foot masseuse his whole life, always hoping that his son would at least be a bricklayer or carpenter. But the son did indeed learn to be a bricklayer or carpenter, and always hoped that in the next life he wouldn't do the same old thing, that rowing a sampan or pulling a rickshaw would be much more enjoyable.

Su Dongpo, the inventor of the Four Joy Meatballs, had these two lines in his bathing-the-baby poem: "I only hope that my son will be foolish and dull, and that he will become a high official without disaster or difficulty." Even a big shot like Su Dongpo complained so much about being an official that he hoped his son would be foolish and dull, not showing the "doing one thing, complaining about it" face like his father. The so-called "becoming a high official without disaster or difficulty" is just saying the same old thing, just talking. Think about it, even the wise and intelligent Su Dongpo had thirty-six disasters and seventy-two difficulties. If he were foolish and dull, how could he ever hope to become a high official? So a great literary figure said, "Not like his father, not like his mother, but like the old shoemaker next door." These are the words in Su Dongpo's heart, but he couldn't write them down, so he deliberately set up a puzzle for later generations to ponder. "However," "not so," to bring the conversation back around. There are many exceptions.

For example, the old man is the "True Son of Heaven." Although this Son of Heaven has reached the point of "wiping away tears to leave the palace" and "hanging himself on Coal Hill," he still hopes that his son will work hard to revive the dynasty, revitalize the old business, and ascend the dragon throne again. So our little brother Puyi, though he became the last emperor of the Qing dynasty, was still desperately trying to be a puppet emperor. And those who are thieves will not "do one thing, complain about it." When a robber is taken to the execution ground, after having his fill of wine and meat, he still shouts, "Twenty years from now, I'll be a good man again." It is known that being a robber is just as enjoyable as being an emperor.

"Dragons beget dragons, phoenixes beget phoenixes, thieves raise sons to dig holes in walls." "Passing down the mantle," "inheriting the family business," only emperors and thieves do that. Other than that, whether learning martial arts to sell one's strength or learning literature to sell one's pen, "not being able to eat enough, starving to death," one can't help but "do one thing, complain about it."

□□ Abandoned 175

— Fei Wenbao

Since the loss of Yuguan, the fall of Rehe, and the simultaneous abandonment of various passes along the Great Wall, the military authorities, to preserve military secrets, have replaced place names with □□. The war news has increased quite a bit □□. A humorist said: □□, the shape is like a square frame, should be read as "kuang" (frame). Now the situation in eastern Luan is critical, □□　　, and it will be abandoned, so it becomes □□ abandoned, □□ abandoned, □□ abandoned. Reading the sound, it is like the sound of cymbals, which is more alarming than the Yuyang war drum. But the gentlemen and ladies in the south, hearing it, do not listen, and dance and sing wildly, with many being like sparrows in a hall, unaware of the impending disaster. Alas! (But reward)

Modern 176

— Zhang Yian

I am not opposed to "modern" (摩登), because "modern" is just a transliteration of the English word "modern." It is a word that existed hundreds of years ago, and its original meaning is "contemporary" or "recent." If used as a noun, it means "a modern person" or "a person with modern ideas." Since we were born as modern people, we are already modern in fact, so why debate it? Some people are intimidated by these two characters, whose meaning cannot be derived from their literal components, and become fascinated by them. Thus, the word "modern" has almost independently acquired a separate meaning in China. In their view, "modern" is not only "new-fashioned," but also contains a certain amount of mystery and romance, and seems to be more closely related to women. As soon as the word "modern" is mentioned, the image that appears in their minds is a woman with short, permed hair, wearing red lipstick, having shaved off her eyebrows and redrawn them with artificial strokes, sticking out her chest, wearing narrow-sleeved, long gowns, and wearing high-heeled leather shoes with silk stockings underneath. And such women also believe that this is what it means to be modern, at most adding some decorative skills, such as dancing and speaking a few common English phrases. I believe that everything modern, from politics to toilet paper 丨 as long as it is a domestic product 丨 should be modern. It is even more natural for women to be modern. A truly modern woman should at least know how to be a housewife who is beneficial to her family, a mother who is beneficial to her children, and a person who is beneficial to society. All of these require the most modern methods. If one only cares about decoration and social activities, then one is truly not worthy of discussing the Way of Modernity.

Since the word "modern" has become popular, there have been speculators in the market who have used this name to speculate, no different from using "curvaceous beauty," "model," and "sensuality" to make profits in the past. I feel quite uneasy about this, so I'm saying a few words.

A Red Sandalwood Tree in Pingwang Town 177

— Yi Mei

"Red beans grow in the south, In spring, how many branches will sprout? I advise you to pick them in plenty, For they will rouse fond love." This short poem by a Tang poet has elevated the value of red beans. The Red Sandalwood Villa of Qian Muzhai in Changshu is especially well-known. There is one in my southern Jiangsu Zen temple, said to have been planted by the Song Dynasty White Pigeon Zen Master, and it is now withered. Behind the Jijian Temple in Tianchi Mountain, Baima Ravine, there is a very large red sandalwood tree, which bears fruit once every few years. The monks of the temple collect the abundant red beans and give them to benefactors to seek incense money. Those devout Buddhist old women often inlay them into hairpins and insert them into their hair, saying that they can ward off evil spirits. There is also one inside the Renxing Pawnshop of Wu Yachang, Fengmen, which is from before the Hong-Yang Rebellion. The pawnshop was originally set up by the Xu family of Wuzhen. The site was originally owned by my relative Peng. During the turmoil of the Hong-Yang Rebellion, Peng Boyun gave the house to others due to lack of funds. This red sandalwood tree has a trunk that one cannot embrace, and its slanting branches extend out of the wall, covering the eaves of the neighbor's house, so when it bears fruit, it often falls down due to the wind, and the neighbor gets an unexpected harvest.

In the dowry of a Jing person, there is a red bean, a product of Tianchi Mountain. When He'er was born, it was inlaid into an ornament and tied around her wrist. Unexpectedly, He'er gnawed it off when her milk teeth first sprouted. I wrote an article at the time called "A Very Regrettable Red Bean," which was published in a certain newspaper. My friend Gu Jundao saw it and generously sent me by mail one of the two red beans produced in the South Pacific Islands that he had collected. That red bean was bright in color and had a precious luster. I treasured it carefully, regarding it as a precious jade.

Zhao Junzhenchu came from Pingwang and saw my red bean. He mentioned the Yuanlai Native Produce Store in Pingwang Town, which has an iron tree in the courtyard. The iron tree is the common name for the red sandalwood tree. Although the tree has luxuriant branches and leaves, it has never borne fruit. Until last autumn, it suddenly bore abundant fruit, harvesting about a few liters. This spring, it was still being distributed to relatives and friends. It is said that the grains are very large and the color is also very lovely.

Long Fiction

Four Company Commanders of the Northeast 178

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Four

The Passionate Situation Reopens in the Teahouse

A Year-End Crisis: The Pawnshop Echoes with Lamentations

There was also money owed to the oil and salt store, the firewood shop, the thread shop. Ordinarily, they didn't take credit; it was a great favor if they extended credit. Now, they felt obliged to pay them back. From early morning, she slowly dealt with the creditors, but by three or four in the afternoon, as it was getting dark, there were still two debts unpaid. One was to the water carrier, less than a dollar, and the other was to the sesame seed cake shop, including sesame cakes eaten and flour borrowed, totaling two dollars. How could she not pay them? The water carrier had come three times that afternoon, which was tolerable. But the most troublesome was the young apprentice from the sesame cake shop, who came countless times. Finally, he stood in the courtyard and said, "Our boss says, are you going to pay or not? If you don't pay, I'll wait here and not go back." Guizhi, being young, still cared about appearances, so she said to Jiang: "It's only two or three dollars, why let this kid shout in the courtyard? Let's take two pieces of clothing to pawn for a few dollars and get rid of these two creditors." Jiang said, "We're wearing all the cotton clothes. The unlined and lined clothes aren't worth much." Guizhi said, "Then I'll take off this cheongsam. I can wear a short jacket. You can wear that thin cotton coat. That tattered leather jacket can also be pawned. We can sleep on the heated kang, and mother and daughter can share one quilt. The mattress can also be taken. Altogether, we should get more than two taels of silver." Jiang thought for a moment and nodded, "That's the only way." So Guizhi, without hesitation, changed her clothes. She pulled the mattress out from under the quilt, rolled up the two pieces of clothing into a large bundle, tucked it under her arm, walked into the courtyard, pointed at the young apprentice and said, "You wait here. It's only two or three dollars, do you have to force people to death?" Saying this, she went to the pawnshop in a huff. In this small town of Haidian, there was indeed a pawnshop. During this time of year, the business was as prosperous as any other store. Guizhi walked into the shop and pushed the bundle onto the counter. The clerk, seeing the items, knew she was a distressed customer because the clothes were still warm. (46)

The US Silver Issue and Inflation Plans 181

President Undecided on Silver Bill

Amendment to Agricultural Relief Act Fails

Washington, April 17th: The Senate today abandoned the proposal to fix silver coinage at a ratio of 16:1 to gold, after hearing that President Roosevelt did not support it. Democratic leader Senator Robinson informed the Senate that the President was undecided on opposing the Silver and Inflation Bill. Senator Wheeler revived the Coinage Bill to aid the Agricultural Relief Act, but Senator Robinson again announced that President Roosevelt hoped that the amendment concerning inflation in the Agricultural Relief Act would fail. The silver amendment to the Agricultural Relief Act ultimately failed by a vote of 43 to 33.

Boisterous Conditions on Reopening Day 183

Silver Dollar Receipts and Payments are Frequent: Guangdong Copper Coins Rise Gradually

Yesterday was the day banks reopened. Foreign banks on the Bund had to process all the receipts and payments that had accumulated during the four-day closure, making it an exceptionally busy day. The surplus or deficiency in funds was not easily calculated, leading to a sharp increase in the water head price. It initially reached 1.2-1.3 cents, then 1.8-1.9 cents, and even 2 cents, before slightly falling back to 1.4-1.5 cents at the close. The price of silver dollars also increased accordingly. The morning and afternoon markets were both at 6 cents. The morning trading volume for short-term bills was over 5.4 million, and the afternoon volume was over 900,000. The trading volume in the Small General Association was over 400,000. Banks' receipts and payments for foreign banks totaled 8.67 million for silver and 9.56 million for silver dollars. Silver dollars entering warehouses amounted to 1.2 million. Chinese banks' receipts and payments for bill payments totaled 5.23 million for silver dollars, and receipts and payments for various cargo, exchange tax, and miscellaneous deposits totaled 14.45 million. Silver dollars entering warehouses amounted to 600,000. Money houses' receipts and payments for silver dollar public notes totaled over 45.5 million. Receipts and payments for water head money totaled 8.34 million. In addition, there were over 10 million in mutual inflows and outflows of silver between the reserve treasury and the money industry. Banknote inflows and outflows amounted to over 2 million. Silver dollar collateral transactions totaled over 2 million.
