A Glimpse of the Bleak Cocoon Market 184

According to financial circles yesterday, in previous years, around this time in late spring, new cocoons from various regions would be successively released onto the market, and the demand for silver dollars in Shanghai would be frequent. However, this year, the opposite is true. The demand for slight special-purpose silver dollars is not strong, and there are virtually no cocoon payments being loaded out. The reasons for this are: First, the weather is too cold, and the development of silkworm moths is incomplete. Natural sericulture is also inferior, not to mention the cocoons of farmers and merchants. Second, the silk market was poor last year, and general traders are reluctant to take risks for meager profits. Third, silver money houses are cautious in lending, especially strict for cocoon lending. At this time of uneven financial adjustment, who would be willing to spend huge sums to purchase cocoons? Therefore, observing from various perspectives, the cocoon market is not only inferior, but may also have to be abandoned invisibly, and no one is willing to do it.

Free Talk

Exposing the Bottom 196

— He Jia Gan

It's good to be thorough in everything, but "exposing the bottom" isn't necessarily brilliant. Because a series of left turns results in encountering friends turning right, at that time, nodding in agreement, your face will feel burning. People who want freedom suddenly want to protect the freedom of restoration, or the freedom to massacre the masses, revealing everything to the bottom, but even the freedom itself is lost, leaving only a bottomless pit.

For example, opposing the eight-legged essay is extremely necessary. The eight-legged essay is originally the product of stupidity. Firstly, the examiners find it troublesome -- most of their brains are made of submerged wood. What kind of representation of sages, what kind of beginning, development, turn, and conclusion, the rhythm of the essay, there are no fixed standards, difficult to grasp. Therefore, it is defined in stocks and shares, considered to conform to the format of official orders. Using this format to "weigh articles", one can see the amount of importance at a glance. Secondly, even the candidates find it very effortless and less troublesome. Such an eight-legged essay, whether old or new, should be swept away. But this is for the sake of being clever, not for being more stupid.

However, there is a strategy to preserve stupid people. They say, "I'm not good, and he's the same as me" -- if everyone can't survive, let's fail together! After "he" fails, the old, stupid "me" always secretly stands up again. The actual benefits belong to the stupid. It's like wanting to overthrow idols. The idols become anxious and point to all the living people saying, "They are all like me". Then you rush to overthrow all the living people who look like idols. When you come back, the idols will give you a reward, saying that overthrowing idols by overthrowing the "overthrowers" is extremely thorough. In fact, at this time, greater stupidity envelops the whole world.

Opening your mouth with poetry, saying "Yu said", this is the old eight-legged essay. And some people consider "Darwin said, Plekhanov said" as the new eight-legged essay. So, to know that the Earth is round, everyone has to travel around the Earth themselves. To manufacture steam engines, one must first sit in front of a boiling kettle to investigate things. This is naturally extremely thorough. In fact, the previous opposition to the literature of defending the Way originally meant that such a man-eating "Way" should not be defended. But some people want to be thorough and say that they don't defend any Way. Isn't this "defending no Way" also a kind of "Way"? Therefore, the truly thorough thing is still the following story:

In ancient times, there was a revolution in a kingdom. The old government fell, and the new one stood up. Others said, "You revolutionaries originally opposed the idea of having a government, how come you yourselves are now running the government?" The revolutionary immediately drew his sword and cut off his own head. However, his body did not fall, but turned into a zombie, standing upright, with his throat seemingly saying haltingly: the realization of this doctrine originally had to wait three thousand years.

Collapse 197

— Luo Hong

Putting down the telephone receiver, he couldn't suppress the trembling of the muscles on his face, couldn't hide his ashen complexion. After mumbling a few words to the people in front of him, he walked out of the manager's office of the rice shop. He had originally wanted to instruct a few people in the accounting room, but he swallowed his words. Stepping onto the hired car, he simply waved to the driver, A Er, and didn't feel like saying anything.

"There's a telegram from Shanghai, things are terrible." This sentence kept ringing in his heart. In the mid-spring weather, the sun shone brilliantly on him, but he felt as if someone had splashed cold water all over him, and he felt strangely cold. The echo of the driver pulling the car rang as arrogantly as usual, and he subconsciously stepped on the foot bell. However, everything in front of him seemed to be collapsing in his eyes. He felt that sitting in the hired car wasn't as imposing as it used to be.

He was thinking vaguely, the car seemed to be pulling faster than usual, and it had already stopped at his door. Walking into the living room, Lao Zhou was waiting with an impatient look. "How bad is it?" he asked, his eyes gleaming.

"The margin money and cotton yarn we speculated on have fallen, a total of 340,000. The market has changed too much, we just can't keep up," said one, shaking his head.

"Then let's give it another shot, do or die, we can't worry about so much," he felt a sense of revulsion rising in his heart.

"It's no good, given the current situation, we can't turn around anymore. If we do it again, I won't do it. I've seen through it. Big players can make fools of us, and we small capital holders can only somersault in their hands. I understand this change completely."

He was silenced. These words cooled his courage. Splitting the loss with Lao Zhou, each of them lost 170,000. After deducting the 50,000 yuan deposit, they still owed 120,000. Looking at Lao Zhou, Lao Zhou's long face was also tense, and he lowered his head, calculating in his mind. The capital of the rice shop and silk shop was exactly 120,000. The family property left by his ancestors, his management of more than ten years, was all gone in an instant. His arrogance and prestige in this city also vanished in an instant. He also secretly blamed himself in his heart for not engaging in this kind of thing and making himself suffer, but he immediately defended himself, besides this, there was no more enjoyable thing. The city was stretching out its hands to tempt people, how would he know that there were large assets at play?

"Do you know? The backers of those big shots are foreigners. Think about it carefully, it's really sad, everything about the Chinese is held in the hands of foreigners," Lao Zhou broke the silence.

"You're not going to empty your pockets, are you? I'm finished," he shook his head, as if seeing his rice shop and silk shop being taken over by others, and even the echo of the hired car didn't sound as loud as before.

Occasionally a spring breeze blew on his face, and he took a deep breath.

Random Notes from My Hometown 198

— Mu Shiying

One, On the Ship

The few small houses in my home have been locked up for eight years -- I miss my hometown so much -- the orange tree in the courtyard, the camellias and irises planted in front of the courtyard, the dim paper windows, the green moss in the pond in front of the door: often causing a faint longing in my heart. This time during the spring break, my father insisted that I go back with my uncle to sweep the tombs, he said:

"If you don't go back, I'm afraid you won't even recognize your ancestors' graves. Fallen leaves return to their roots, and one day you will always go back."

I then understood that this was hereditary, the homesickness of the race, so I picked up a suitcase, brought a cane, jumped on the ship, together with a light soul.

The ship was terribly crowded that day, with people lying everywhere. So many people! They were all speaking the intimate local language. They cursed people with the most vulgar words. They were all simple, innocent big children. They loved to speak local dialects, loved to boast. So I looked at them and smiled. I was happy because our fellow villagers were accustomed to speaking local dialects, bragging, and cursing people with all sorts of words that no one could imagine. Sometimes their boasting would get to the point where even they themselves couldn't believe it. They would curse to the point where even their own children couldn't help but laugh. They were all lovable people! They grew up in the same soil as me. They were a fish-and-salt-eating people, and I was also a fish-and-salt-eating person.

When the ship set sail, I leaned against the iron railing on the deck, looked at the shadows of the clouds in the river, and dreamed of my hometown. The bow slowly turned sideways, and I heard the river slapping against the hull of the ship, so I said, "Goodbye, Shanghai! Our hometown is the land of fish and salt, our hometown has truly clear blue skies, green waters, white clouds. Our hometown is such a simple and unadorned land! We are going home!" So I thought.

The antennas of the tall buildings stretched out, always stretching out, but slowly the wind flags of the Jianghai Customs disappeared, the clock disappeared, the golden dome of the Sassoon Building disappeared, followed by countless warehouses, getting a little bigger, then a little smaller, smaller. The tall smokestacks of the power plant were as small as a bunch of pencils. When the first sea breeze blew my hair up after leaving the Wusongkou, I gently shouted: "Go, Shanghai!" I was drunk.

At night, the waves were terrible, hitting the bottom of the ship with a bang. I quietly lay in bed and watched the swaying of the silk ribbon of the gauze curtain, unable to fall asleep. How could I fall asleep? When it dawned, I would be in my hometown. At four o'clock in the morning, I quietly got up, lit a cigarette, and secretly ran to the deck. Looking out, it was all boundless blue water. On that endless surface of the water, the light of the lighthouse floated, shining far away, following the waves, disappearing for a while, and then reappearing. I stared blankly at the lighthouse. This was more beautiful than the New Year's red lanterns. Life was so changing, and life was such a monotonous cycle. I don't know how many. In the gray dawn, a black line of land appeared at the horizon. Slowly the black line got closer, clearer, and I could see the trees, fields, and distant shadows of mountains above. Suddenly I jumped up as if mad, struggled for a long time, and then sat back on the canvas chair, sighing: "I'm here! That's my hometown!"

On the Way Home (Continued) 199

— Liu Ceng

The two foreigners seemed a little embarrassed. I can very well understand this embarrassment. A year ago, when traveling with my wife in small cities or rural areas in foreign countries, wasn't I often stared at by many people?

Probably because I was the only one wearing Western clothes in the car, the two foreigners seemed to be waiting for me to turn around. As soon as our eyes met, one of the foreigners asked me in English:

"Is Minhang up ahead?"

"Please ask me in Chinese. I can't speak English." During the years in Europe, seeing many British people, no matter what country they were in, as soon as they encountered a yellow person, especially a Chinese person, they would rudely and without regard for the situation, address you directly in English, as if all Chinese people had received colonial education and should be able to speak a few words of English. This made me have a deep aversion, and whenever British or Americans treated me as a "superior Chinese person" and tried to chat with me in English, I would immediately throw these words back at them.

"Aren't you speaking English right now?" Another foreigner laughed.

"I can only speak this sentence," I also laughed. "If you can speak French, please talk in French. Then it will be more convenient for everyone."

Most British and American youths who have received a university education can speak a few words of French. So the two foreigners talked to me in French that was barely intelligible.

These were two young Canadian travelers. They planned to stay in Shanghai for a month or two. They heard that Minhang was very close to Shanghai, and they wanted to play for half a day, hoping to see something novel. Foreigners are very curious.

"Are you going to Minhang too?" One of the foreigners asked, looking at the bouquet in my hand.

"No, I'm getting off here."

"Does your home live here?"

"Yes."

The car happened to stop at this time, and the driver called loudly: "XX Cemetery".

"Isn't there just a cemetery here?" One of the foreigners asked, his eyes widened.

"Yes. But my woman lives here." I said, holding the bouquet, and got out of the car.

X X X X

Amidst the caretaker's joyful cry of "The gentleman has come again", I walked into the cemetery.

This is now my wife's home, which is also my future home. Next to where my wife is sleeping peacefully, isn't there a vacant lot left?

Crossroads of Era and Love 200

Talks

A Gathering of Heroes 201

— Bao Fu

Recently, the frontline battles have failed to capture the attention of the people of our country. The eyes of our countrymen have all turned to Washington, across the ocean, watching the new play about to be staged in Washington. Haven't the selections for representatives to the Washington Conference been a clamorous topic domestically these past few days? The names "Minister Song" and "President Sun" have been the subject of enough noise here. Now, after "careful" consideration by the government and "humble" deferrals by "the individuals themselves," it has been decided that Minister Song will take the stage. In the near future, Minister Song will set sail, playing a role in the Washington Conference.

The Washington Conference is convened by the newly elected President of the United States, Mr. Roosevelt. The invited countries are a select few powerful nations. Small countries are naturally excluded (China, surprisingly, is also invited, gaining a place among the ranks of the powerful, which is truly an honor). The representatives of each participating country are mostly powerful and top-tier figures, fully capable of representing their respective countries' will, such as the British Prime Minister MacDonald, the former French Prime Minister Herriot, the Italian Minister of Finance Jung, and the Japanese diplomatic elder statesman Ishii Kikujiro, all of whom are outstanding talents and heroes of their time. This conference is truly nothing less than a "gathering of heroes" from the great powers.

So, what will this "gathering of heroes" discuss? The scope of discussion is not small: the entire war debt problem, the World Economic Conference, tariff policies, international exchange rates, world trade, disarmament issues, and the general global situation, among other things. As for the Far East issue, which is closely related to our country, it is said that it is also "planned" to be discussed. Precisely because we heard that "the Sino-Japanese issue will also be 'planned' to be discussed," the people of our country are craning their necks, hoping that this conference will provide a fair judgment and forceful sanctions on the Sino-Japanese problem. Our government is also paying special attention to the selection of representatives for this reason.

The outcome of the talks is, of course, beyond our ability to predict. However, it is absolutely impossible for the Sino-Japanese problem to advance towards resolution during these talks. Even if progress is made, it may not be beneficial to us. We should not be deluded by Roosevelt's slogan of promoting international cooperation. This so-called "international" is merely the international of imperialist countries, and the so-called cooperation is merely the alliance of imperialists. This is evident from the fact that socialist Soviet Russia and other small countries have not been invited.

Soviet Russia is their common enemy. The main purpose of this conference is to prepare a united front against their common enemy and to lay the foundation for a capitalist anti-Soviet alliance. To lay a solid front, they must first resolve the deep-seated panic they share, so economic issues become the theme of discussion. To achieve consistent unity, they must temporarily eliminate the conflicts within imperialism itself, so international cooperation becomes the slogan. Didn't Roosevelt hint at abandoning the United States' eight-year-old policy of diplomatic isolation? This fully proves that the United States has decided to join the anti-Soviet front. Anglo-American cooperation will be promoted during this conference, and the conflict between Japan and the United States will also be eased. If Anglo-American cooperation succeeds, Britain's war debts may not become a major international problem for the time being. If the conflict between Japan and the United States temporarily disappears, it will inevitably lead to the United States recognizing Japan's position in the Far East. The most fundamental and acute opposition in the world is between Britain and the United States, and between Japan and the United States. If these two oppositions can be temporarily eased, the anti-Soviet front can be formed. This is the fundamental goal of this conference. Therefore, under these circumstances, the Far East issue has become a key to achieving their goals. In this way, is China's hopeful anticipation of a fair judgment not a dream!

Literature and Art

Our country has always adhered to peace, and the loss of the four northeastern provinces under the policy of non-resistance has prompted these four poems on objects, with deep feeling.

Ode to the Pig

Stupid, foolish, fat and healthy, breathing heavily,

Approaching slaughter, with no plan to flee.

The principle remains non-resistance,

Allowing blood to smear the ground mercilessly.

Ode to the Sheep

Three hundred sheep, united in heart,

Sudden foreign calamity tears them apart.

The principle remains non-resistance,

Wolves devour them, a disaster to impart.

Ode to the Ox

Farm families tend fields with diligence,

Yet draped in colorful robes, temples appear for reverence.

The principle remains non-resistance,

Knowing not return, recognizing nothing beyond offense.

Ode to the Horse

A herd known for generations in the northern region,

Saddled and ridden, enduring a life of submission.

The principle remains non-resistance,

A confused mix of good and ill-intention.

Shanghai Morning Talk 202

— Xian

The Old Master and Madam

The Old Master and Madam are the protagonists of Shanghai night talks. In Shanghai morning talks, aside from the brief appearances of those returning from dance halls, exhausted from dancing, being carried from cars into small Western-style houses, the Old Master and Madam mentioned here are naturally different people, sleeping soundly on wild duck down mattresses, seeking sweet dreams. If you don't believe me, please read on.

My home is in a very bustling alley along the road. All kinds of noisy sounds, whether from inside the alley or from the road, are clearly delivered to our ears all day long. There is no peace and quiet during the day, and one cannot sleep peacefully at night. The quietest time of day is usually when I return from work. It usually doesn't seem to be a problem for me, but as soon as dawn breaks, the Shanghai people's experienced and high-pitched voices scream from the hoarse throats of the Old Master and Madam. The maids and horses neigh loudly. My tired body cannot help but curse them in the position of a petty bourgeois, scolding them for disturbing my peaceful dreams, for being tasteless things! When the red sun sets in the west, I get out of bed again, and I can't help but think, what am I working so hard for every day? The Old Master and Madam are the same as me. Their hoarse voices are like my hands, and their high-pitched screams are like the words I write. I have to eat, don't they have to eat? I have to sleep peacefully, don't they sleep peacefully? Aren't they afraid of the oppression of early frost and cold dew? Regardless of the cold or heat, it's like this every day, every year, without rest, working hard, for the sake of a few cents of income every day, going back to support the old and raise the young, sustaining the family's life. If they don't work for a day, they don't eat for a day. So often, from the days of "tipping" young masters and daughters, until they become Old Master and Madam, they are still doing the hard work of the "tipping" generation. They never have good food, good clothes, or good housing. The mark of their life becomes a hoarse voice, still "tipping," "tipping," reaching the end of their lives.

Although they do such dirty work, can we do without them? How many people living in Shanghai have big houses with flush toilets? Because they do dirty work, they are despised by gentlemen and adults, but if Shanghai didn't have them, do the Old Master and Madam who sit in cars and dance know what kind of world Shanghai would become?

Relying on one's own strength, eating one's own food, this is exactly the kind of talent needed today!

I rub my shy eyelids and don't curse them for being tasteless things just because I haven't woken up. After hurriedly smoking a cigarette, I drag my heavy footsteps, using my hands to grab what I eat, wear, and live on.

But at this time, it is almost evening, and the Old Master and Madam are dressed neatly to pursue their pleasures in a snow-white 1933 Austin, with new clothes made of silk and satin, chasing each other in the neon lights.

I bury myself in the pile of drafts, looking at the clock on the wall, wondering if I can go home a little earlier today, before the Old Master and Madam start working.

Arithmetic

A Simple Method for Converting Between Taels and Dollars 203

Having read Mr. Yongxiang's "Another Quick Method for Correcting the Conversion of Two Dollars," which can calculate up to the hundred-thousandth place and is extremely accurate, I find that the mnemonic is quite complex and not easy to memorize. At the beginning of the change from taels to dollars, I created a "Flying Return Mnemonic for Taels to Dollars Conversion," which is simple, easy to remember, and accurate even when calculating to the ten-millionth or hundred-millionth place. Now, I will record my Chinese mnemonic below:

Page 16

Mnemonic

For two, add one, two eight five

For two, add two, add five seven

For three, add four, add one four

For four, add five, four two five

For five, add six, add seven one

For six, add eight, add two eight

For seven, add nine, five six five

For eight, add ten, subtract one five

Algorithm: Similar to ordinary division, from left to right, but in ordinary division, division is always followed by division. This method always follows division with an addition. Only the last sentence of the mnemonic is a divisor. For example, "For one, add one, two eight five." If the first digit of the number is one, remove one from that digit, add one to the digit above it, and add two eight five from the digit below it. The rest is analogous. The second half of the first seven sentences of the mnemonic are all addition numbers. The use or non-use of the word "add" is to make the sentence surface neat and easy to read aloud, so it has nothing to do with the algorithm. Only the last sentence, "add ten," must be paid attention to, as it adds one to the digit two places above the original digit. If you encounter eight, add nine, you can calculate it with the last sentence of the mnemonic and then treat the remainder as one and return it with the first sentence of the mnemonic. If the remainder is two or three, return it with the second or third sentence of the mnemonic. The numbers "add one" and "add two" are the quotients, and the addition numbers in the second half of the sentence are the remainders. The reason for not creating a mnemonic for encountering eight or nine is that the more mnemonics there are, the harder they are to memorize. For example, encountering one can also create a mnemonic "For one, add two, subtract four three." Encountering two can also create a mnemonic "For two, add three, subtract one four five." When there is something to subtract, it is very convenient, but when there is nothing to subtract, it is not applicable. Now there is a sentence "For seven, add ten, subtract one five" to adjust it. Other division mnemonics can also be omitted together. After the method is completely calculated, the unit of the quotient is one digit before the unit of the divisor. This is the simplest and most accurate method I have learned through experience. I record it to await the correction of arithmetic experts. As for the method of converting dollars to taels, my proposed method is consistent with that written by Mr. Yongxiang, so I will not repeat it.

Shop Assistant Correspondence 205

A Maid with No Pay

Editor Sir:

I am a weak woman, who came here at the age of seven, and it has been eleven years now. My status is nominally an adopted daughter, but in fact, I am a "maid with no pay." In the past eleven years, the suffering I have endured is truly beyond words. Recently, life has become even more unbearable, and I have to do everything myself. But after working like a beast of burden all year round, the price I get, besides a few old clothes that can barely cover my body, and three meals a day of leftovers, is only "swallowing my anger" and "being scolded." I have long wanted to escape this environment, but I have never had the opportunity. Two years ago, I was fortunate enough to meet a man three years older than me; he also loves me very much. In these two years, we have come to know each other: so it is only natural to want to marry. I also know that the best way is to ask my master to fulfill our wish. But he is of course also considered to be a lowly person by the general public, so how can he have such connections? Besides, my master is treating me as a field that has already been plowed, so how can he agree to it? Unable to do so, I thought of the next best thing, so I asked him to elope with me; but he is, after all, a good person: afraid of violating the law, so he dared not try it for a while. Sir, if I really eloped with him, would it implicate him? Besides this, is there any other way for me to achieve the life I want? Please give me a detailed answer within the next two or three days. I am sincerely looking forward to it here! I wish you

Good Health, Shen Suzhen

X X X X

Editor's Note: Although the above letter has undergone considerable modification by us, the original letter is still able to express its meaning. For a woman who has been an adopted daughter since she was a child, to be able to have such accomplishments, her master does not seem to be very vicious. Therefore, in this matter, we still advocate explaining it to Ms. Shen's master. You can tell them this idea yourself, without necessarily having to find a third party to convey the message. You might as well say, "My mind is made up, even if you don't agree, I will definitely do this." It would be best if they could meet the trend and allow your request. If they don't, contrary to your expectations, and refuse to let you go, then you can ask a lawyer to dissolve your relationship with them first, which is easy to do丨Then marry your partner. "Elopement" is really not a good idea, implicating him and subjecting him to the law is of course inevitable; and once you run away, your lives will definitely be threatened丨Please think twice before you act丨

Fiction

Passing Time in a Dream (32 Continued) 206

— Qin Shouou

He was thinking hard, praying bitterly, hoping that he could hook and safely rescue Wang Guodong, who had committed public anger. Because he was thinking too hard, his nerves had temporarily changed, causing him to stand there vaguely for a long time without returning to his seat. Fortunately, he was the leader of the whole school. Although people noticed, no one interfered. Moreover, most of the participants were listening quietly to the chairman's report on the stage with bated breath, and had no time to pay attention to the headmaster's change of behavior. However, he did not hear a single sentence of the chairman's report on the stage. When he gradually calmed down, he only heard the people under the stage straightening their voices and shouting desperately:

"Severely punish the greedy and traitorous Wang Guodong!"

"Expel Wang Guodong, who damaged the reputation of the whole school!"

Among them, there was also a group of radical elements roaring angrily.

"Quick, tie him up and parade him through the streets!"

"Punish him to stand in a wooden cage for half a month!"

Finally, many young people with the most intense emotions actually raised their thick arms, glared their terrible eyes, and squeezed together to rush to the stage to take action.

Wang Guodong was in a situation of being besieged on all sides. He wanted to escape but could not, he wanted to beg for mercy but it was useless. Seeing that he was about to suffer a big loss, he tightly protected his head with his two arms, squatted down halfway, and his teeth were clattering, almost scared to death.

"Now everyone's opinions are almost the same! We must not simply expel this shameless thing. We must punish him severely. Well, let's discuss the method of punishment丨" From the presidium, a person with a very loud voice and a very brave attitude came out, stopped everyone's confusion, and said a few words to summarize the outline.

Wu Yi took a closer look and realized that the speaker was his son, Wu Yuan.

"He must be punished to stand in a wooden cage for a month!"

"Compel his family to donate 10,000 yuan to the volunteer army as atonement!"

"Starting tomorrow, make him publish in the newspaper for ten days, confessing his crimes!"

Although the emergency action was stopped by Wu Yuan, the methods of punishment proposed by all parties became more and more fierce. Some even advocated sending Wang Guodong to the garrison headquarters to be shot according to the law. Just as they were arguing, Wu Yi had moved his steps and walked to the podium.

"Listen to Principal Wu's opinion"! Liu Ji, the executive committee member of the Student Anti-Japanese Association who was standing in the center, thought that Wu Yi also had some opinions on punishing Wang Guodong, so he shouted, making everyone under the stage stop speaking, so that he could speak.

"Chairman, may I ask what Wang Guodong has done wrong?" Wu Yi was determined to defend Wang Guodong and had to first find out the cause.

"Principal丨Didn't you hear our report just now?" Liu Ji showed a very surprised look, reluctantly enduring, and repeated: "Wang Guodong is the director of the inspection team of the Anti-Japanese Association, and he bears a great responsibility. Unexpectedly, the Student Union sent someone to warn us recently, saying that not only was our inspection ineffective, but also someone had been bribed by unscrupulous merchants and secretly issued those seals of "already inspected" covers, so that Japanese goods could still be sold smoothly. After we received this warning, we investigated strictly, and we found out that Wang Guodong had done a good thing alone丨"

"Is there any evidence?" Wu Yi questioned.

"How can there be no丨" Liu Ji expressed great dissatisfaction with Wu Yi's questioning. "We have arrested two owners of foreign sundry goods stores, and they have all confessed. Even Wang Guodong himself does not deny it丨Therefore, we only need to discuss how to punish him now丨"

As soon as Liu Ji finished speaking, several other students crowded around two middle-aged men who looked like merchants, squeezing to Wu Yi's face, meaning: "The witnesses are all here, don't believe you ask yourself丨" With such corroboration, even if Wang Guodong's father丨Wang Yulin, a lawyer who has been in practice for more than 20 years, came to defend him in person, it would be impossible to recover. Not to mention Wu Yi, who is not good at eloquence丨

"Well::, then let's just expel him丨" Wu Yi planned to allow the expulsion of Wang Guodong to ease the atmosphere on the stage.

Film Special

An Analysis of Huaress Pylath's Success 207

— Wen Ying

Attributes Ugly Looks to Be His Main Reason

The face of the great star Huaress Pylath in "Grand Hotel" is so ugly that even dogs would run away from it. One can imagine how unattractive his appearance is. But movie fans all over the world find his face lovable. Whether he plays a robber, a thief, a scoundrel, or a hypocrite, they all praise his good performance. Isn't that strange? Here is a passage in which he analyzes his own success. He attributes it to his own ugly appearance. I have seen the portraits of emperors of past dynasties collected in the Qing Palace, some of which are so strangely ugly that they do not resemble human rulers. For example, the appearance of Ming Taizu was like a pig, extremely ugly; but physiognomists said that although this was a pig shape, it was actually born of a pig dragon, which was extremely noble, so he could become the Son of Heaven. Therefore, those with strange and ugly appearances are either extremely lowly or extremely noble. Now this Huaress Pylath, with his big nose, wide mouth slightly protruding forward, also looks somewhat like a pig. Therefore, he was a shepherd boy in his childhood (once herding elephants for others), and now he is a great star, jumping from extreme lowliness to great wealth. I am now translating his words and publishing them in the Shen Bao Film Magazine, to give the ugly people of the world a chance to vent their anger. (The following is Pylath's own speech)

"You ask me how I became famous? Even I myself don't know. If I knew, I would definitely tell you. (He squinted at himself from a mirror on the wall of the dressing room and continued) Maybe it's because my appearance is too outrageous! I don't think there is any other reason besides that. But I really didn't expect my appearance to make a lot of money. However (he was a little shy) I wasn't ugly when I was a kid. Have you seen my childhood photos? Don't look down on me. I even joined a song and dance troupe丨My brother Noah and I performed in a song and dance troupe, and that was the first step I took in acting. Think about what it would be like to see the two of us open our hippopotamus-like mouths, singing and dancing!

"When I paired with other people in plays, the love of the woman always belonged to other people at the end of the play. I wasn't angry either, because that's how it is. With this face, one shouldn't fantasize about winning a woman's love丨

"But when it comes to being ugly, I also have many advantages that pretty boys can't match. First, I don't need makeup. My natural map can be used to my advantage everywhere. Second, I don't need to prop up the scene, because I don't play the roles of upper-class gentlemen. Third, I don't have to worry about my bald head. Fourth, no one laughs at me for picking my teeth in public. Fifth, no one cares if I don't shave for three days. Sixth, I'm not afraid of getting old. People feel the sense of beauty fading when they find a wrinkle on their forehead in the mirror; I'm not afraid, the more wrinkles, the better. As for my hair, I can cut it into a flat top or leave it messy, it's really advantageous everywhere.

"I once argued with Mary Tolan. Although she won at the time, I'm still not convinced to this day. When we were filming Min and Bill, Mary and I argued about who was uglier. I thought I was the ugliest, but she insisted that she was the ugliest. In the midst of the breakup, I had to give in because she was an old lady. In fact, she was just a little older, how could she compare to my ugliness!"

(He stood up and looked at the mirror next to him and said) "I get uglier every year, but the uglier the better丨"

Audience Opinion

A Few Idle Words on "The Ball of Light and Pearl Shadow" 208

— Wei

Yesterday, I watched "The Ball of Light and Pearl Shadow" at "Xin Guang." This morning, I read the review in the Shen Bao film supplement and felt compelled to say a few idle words. Mr. "Ling He" seems to have misunderstood some aspects of the film's story and the motivation and background behind its creation.

Regarding the story: The main point is that the protagonist, based on his own experience, nearly falls into a state of irredeemable depravity due to a single misstep. Seeing that his younger brother is about to repeat his mistake, he devises a plan during a football game to subdue his brother's arrogance, preventing him from succumbing to the temptations of a wicked society. This is truly a lesson in ethical friendship and chivalrous spirit.

As for the motivation: The story of this film merely serves as an interlude. The real motivation for filming it lies in the two football matches. The American people's fervor for college football games has a history of half a century. Every fall and winter, at each college football game in various cities and towns, the number of spectators often reaches one or two hundred thousand, showcasing the grandeur and frenzy. All universities regard recruiting and training elite football teams as the sole means to enhance their school's reputation. Each year, at the end of the football season, a selection of honorary team members for the "All-American Team" and the "All-American Second Team" is held, determined by a judging panel composed of the most prestigious football coaches nationwide. However, matches involving these honorary teams have never been held. The American film industry, discerning the public's psychology, incorporated a scene from the Universal Pictures new film "The Speculative Madam." This film opens today. at the Xin Guang Grand Theater. The female lead is Katie Naje. She previously starred in "The Fairy of Neon Clothes" and "Happy Foes," which were screened in Shanghai. Those who have seen the above two films may not have forgotten the lady's beauty and artistry.

The studio hired players selected for the "All-American Team" in 1930 and 1931 to film the movie. Therefore, the English name remains "All Americans." As for the two brothers who are the protagonists of the film, although they are purely film actors, in reality, they were both renowned football players during their time at school. Furthermore, concerning the background: given the national fervor for football, although university students can gain temporary fame in football or sports while in school, after graduation, they often lack other skills besides sports, ultimately leading to unemployment and depravity. Therefore, the film carries a satirical intent, urging young students not to be blinded by vanity and neglect their studies. The inclusion of women and society in the film is nothing more than to encourage students to be wary of the evils of society, and to increase the interest of the story. Finally, the purpose of my idle words is because I saw that most of the audience yesterday were young students, just like the master in the movie.

"Exploiting the Poor" 209

— Xie Xingguang

Having not set foot inside a theater for two whole months, I could no longer suppress the burgeoning desire to see a play. In the daytime, I fished out the only two dimes in my pocket and headed straight for the "Proletarian XX Grand Theater." Before I knew it, the exterior of the XX Grand Theater, from blurred to distinct, was entirely before my eyes. I fished out the two dimes in my pocket, ready to exchange them for a ticket.

I strode into the theater's entrance and slapped the two dimes onto the ticket window, putting on the pompous air of a patron, and said, "Change!"

"Quite the coincidence!" The ticket seller sized me up for a moment and said.

"It's a big coin!" I said again in surprise.

"It's the theater's rule; large and small coins are used equally."

"Oh! A large coin is the same as a small coin:" I shivered, took the ticket, and walked despondently into the darkened space. The four words "exploiting the poor" surged into my mind.

Editor's Note: I will publish your manuscript; you can see two more movies next month. But it is better to change the money to small coins to prevent being exploited again.

"Oppression" Filming Completed 210

— Jingguan

The Latest Production by Mingxing Company

Recently, the Mingxing Film Company completed another silent film, which was unofficially screened at the Central Grand Theater on the night of the spring rain.

The name of this film is "Oppression." The director is Gao Lihen. The protagonist is a weak-willed worker whose factory is forced to close down due to economic oppression by big capitalists, causing him to lose his job. After losing his job, he can't think of a solution and has to let his wife go out to work as a servant. As a result, his wife is taken away by someone else, and his old mother and daughter die in the snow. Finally, he finds a job, but he is framed again, and eventually goes to prison with lingering grief and hatred. In this film, the hard lives of the so-called lower class are depicted in detail. The leading roles are played by Gong Jianong as the worker and Xia Peizhen as the worker's wife. These two are even more impressive when playing the role of unkempt and poor people than when wearing suits and qipaos. There is also an important female role, played by Yan Yuexian. According to her personality, she naturally plays the role of a fashionable and beautiful socialite in the film.

Seven Companies Join Forces to Film a Patriotic Movie. It is Said That the Government Has Agreed to Assist. 211

— Zong

The "National Salvation Through Aviation," which was heavily promoted in Shanghai, cannot be considered a failure. Now those enthusiasts in the film industry have already had two meetings and decided that the cooperating companies are seven in total. There are three sound film companies:

Film Novel Cavalcade (1) 212

— Ne

"Cavalcade" is produced by the American Fox Company, but the actors and directors, everything is British. This publication has already introduced the production process of "Cavalcade" on the 29th and 30th of last month by Lin Jun. Now, I will ask Ne Jun to excerpt its plot and publish it daily to resonate with readers.

That day was New Year's Eve again. In the Merrio family, Qi Yin and Robert, after ten years of marriage, were as happy as if it were just one day. As usual, at twelve o'clock on New Year's Eve, the couple would raise their glasses to celebrate, to bid farewell to the past year of peace and welcome the birth of a year of peace. But this year was not like the previous years. Today, what was being sent off was not an ordinary year, but a century, because that day was December 31, 1899.

The new century is like a new life. And at the beginning of this new century, Britain had already engaged in war with Dutch farmers stationed in South Africa. Within the new year, Robert had to pack his bags and go to defend his country with arms. Qi Yin was heartbroken at the thought of this. The ten years of harmonious family life had been enveloped by a cold and rainy atmosphere. Her husband had to go on a long expedition, and both of her sons were still young. From then on, the days would only increase her sorrow.

Qi Yin's eyes were filled with tears, and they had not dried for a day. She looked at the pot of flowers given to her by the servants and pointed to her husband, saying, "The smaller the things, the more they move people's hearts. I want to cry." She sobbed, "A few tears to welcome the new century."

Robert held her, and she gained infinite courage. At this time, the distant clock had not yet struck, and this moment still belonged to the old century, the peaceful era that Robert and she shared. She stared at his face and asked, "We have been so happy since we got married!"

"Until now?" Qi Yin also knew the fear in Robert's heart. "Why not leave some leeway for the future?"

Qi Yin cried. "Who knows if there will be a future? Alas, baby, darling, why must you leave me? How can I bear it?"

"The bugle has sounded!" Robert smiled. He had to smile; if he didn't smile, he could only cry with her, because he himself had unresolved bitterness. "The bugle has sounded, the national flag is flying." Then he hummed a military song, "Britons will never be slaves to others."

Automobile News

Williams' New Car Adapts to the New Era 213

Lower Price Than Before, More Perfect Manufacturing Than Before, the Most Ideal, Most Beautiful and Cheapest Car. Times change and things change with them. Today's world can truly be called a new world. Williams Ofrin has seen through the trend of this realistic new world, and began to manufacture 1933-style cars, sweeping away the old atmosphere of the past to adapt to the special economic situation of the time.

When Williams Ofrin Company designed and manufactured the 1933-style car, it was determined to take into account those in society who have reduced their income by more than 50% since 1929. Therefore, the price of the new car must be suitable for the reduced purchasing power, and the beauty of its style and the greatness of its function must not be reduced in the slightest, so that it can be happily used by the most discerning customers. The company also learned that the general purchasing habits of society are completely opposite to those of the past. They often care about how much they spend, and they must get 100 points of value for every yuan they spend, because it is far more difficult to make money than it used to be. Therefore, the company decided that the new car should not only be cheap to buy, but also save on all daily maintenance costs in order to adapt to the purchasing power of the general public.

The Car Style is Unique

The company's 1933 car style has completely changed its old appearance and is brand new. Based on scientific principles and imitating the structure of airplanes, it increases the maximum speed without adding fuel costs, and its body posture is more beautiful than the old style. In short, Williams Ofrin's new car can be called the most complete car with a streamlined design adopted by the general public.

Even its car lights are based on the streamlined style, installed on the protective board and tilted backwards to match the car lines, and the light is radiated directly to the front, and because of the angle of the car lights, the light distribution is more satisfactory.

The Biggest Goal is Economy

The company's biggest goal is to make cars more economical, so the savings in daily maintenance costs are as important as reducing the purchase price. The creation of Williams 77 uses one gallon of American gasoline and can travel 25 to 30 miles, and one gallon of machine oil can travel 1,000 miles, which is clear evidence that the company has achieved its goal. In fact, the company has reduced transportation costs by half, which is consistent with the amount of reduction in public benefits.

Regarding the performance of the new car, the company also knows that in this era, transportation is of utmost importance, so the structure of the new car meets the needs of the most demanding drivers. It can travel 70 miles per hour, and thanks to its patented "buoyancy," it can also be smoother than usual, which is one of its characteristics. Also, the high speed of its second gear ensures smooth operation and rapid movement.

There are Many Features, Roughly Listed Below

The Williams 77 is equipped with a four-cylinder engine that can generate 48 horsepower and 3,200 revolutions per minute. The exhaust valve is in a suitable position, making it convenient for the driver. The piston is made of pig iron and has three compression rings and one oil return ring. The clutch and transmission are old-fashioned. The clutch is made of a whole metal sheet with a diameter of eight inches. The cylinder diameter is nine inches and the width is one inch and six points. Just apply slight pressure on the pedal and the action will follow.

The entire car body is made of pure steel. The car frame uses a double vertical X-style, which is the latest style of car frame. The front and rear are extremely strong. The front and rear seats are quite wide, and the spring cushions are very deep and stable. They are tilted backwards at the correct angle, so they are very comfortable. The front of the 77 sedan has a single seat that can be moved. There is a small drawer next to it for placing scattered packages.

The wheel diameter is seventeen inches, the rim is three inches, and the tire is five inches. The wheels are also manufactured in a streamlined style. The front axle is based on the old-fashioned style, with very little curvature, so the torsion is very strong.

The fire manager is fully automatic. The heat shield can be adjusted at any time. Other equipment such as hydraulic front and rear shock absorbers, non-glare front windows, oil filters, rearview mirrors, rubber pedals, foot accelerator, etc. are all complete.

This is the Crystallization of Twenty-Six Years

This Williams Ofrin 1933 new car is the greatest achievement in its 26-year history. It has exhausted its spirit, financial resources, and all equipment to achieve this success. In a world where economic power is declining, if you want to enjoy a car that meets the needs of the times, where else can you look? Therefore, the above is a brief description of the advantages of its new car, so that those who buy cars know where to ask.

Recent Public Concession 214

Song.

Automobile Registration Statistics

A Total of 8,263 Vehicles

The Shanghai Public Concession's automobile registration statistics for the first quarter of this year have now been released. As of the end of March, there were a total of 8,263 registered vehicles in the concession, including 6,288 private and public automobiles, and 1,977 freight vehicles, trailers, and public buses. In addition to automobile registration, the number of registered motorcycles was 756. However, the above figures do not include all the vehicles used by foreign armies and navies.

In terms of automobile registration, including private, public, and freight vehicles, Ford cars still rank first, with 719 passenger cars and 458 freight cars, totaling 1,177 vehicles. The second-highest number of registered passenger cars is Buick, with 590 vehicles. The third is Austin with 483 vehicles. The fourth is Chevrolet with 461 vehicles. The fifth is Morris Cowley with 330 vehicles. The sixth is Studebaker with 311 vehicles. The seventh is Essex with 306 vehicles. The eighth is Dodge with 255 vehicles. The ninth is Waldorf Gray with 231 vehicles. The tenth is Erskine with 204 vehicles. Nash ranks eleventh with 202 vehicles. Morris Oxford ranks twelfth with 185 vehicles. Citroen ranks thirteenth with 144 vehicles. Chrysler ranks fourteenth with 122 vehicles. Standard ranks fifteenth with 119 vehicles. Morris Minor ranks sixteenth with 108 vehicles. Hupmobile ranks seventeenth with 104 vehicles. Plymouth ranks eighteenth with 103 vehicles.

The number of registered freight vehicles, trailers, and public buses. Ford ranks first with 458 vehicles. The second place is Stewart with 171 vehicles. The third is Chevrolet with 166 vehicles. The fourth is Tilling-Stevens, which are public buses, with 139 vehicles. The fifth place is Studebaker with 94 vehicles. The sixth is Reo with 91 vehicles. The seventh place is MGC with 78 vehicles. The eighth place is Morris with 68 vehicles. The ninth place is Diamond T with 67 vehicles. The tenth place is Donnc Raff with 54 vehicles, of which 11 are public buses. International Harvester ranks eleventh with 46 vehicles. Renault ranks twelfth with 49 vehicles. Leyland ranks thirteenth with 44 vehicles. Dodge ranks fourteenth with 37 vehicles, of which 12 are public buses. Garford ranks fifteenth with 20 vehicles. Citroen ranks sixteenth with 18 vehicles. Waldorf Gray and Le Bette both rank seventeen.
